Case 112-Title: Lemon-Blueberry Cake
Ingredients: ["3 cups flour", "2 cups sugar", "1 teaspoon baking powder", "34 teaspoon baking soda", "12 teaspoon cinnamon", "12 teaspoon salt", "14 teaspoon nutmeg", "1 cup fat-free buttermilk", "3 large eggs", "12 cup canola oil", "1 tablespoon lemon zest (grated)", "12 teaspoon vanilla", "2 cups fresh blueberries"]
Directions: ["Preheat oven to 350F Spray a 10\" Bundt pan with nonstick spray and dust with flour.", "Set aside.", "Mix together flour, sugar, baking powder, baking soda, cinnamon, salt, and nutmeg in a large bowl.", "In a second bowl, whisk together buttermilk, eggs, oil, lemon zest, and vanilla.", "Add buttermilk mixture to flour mixture and stir until just blended.", "Gently stir in the blueberries.", "Pour batter into prepared pan.", "Bake 60-70 minutes, or until a toothpick inserted in the center comes out clean.", "Let cool in the pan for 15 minutes.", "Remove cake and let cool on a rack.", "NOTES: 182 cal, or 4 WW points a serving."]
Requirement: Mustard-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Lemon-Blueberry Cake Recipe (Mustard-Free)**

Ingredients:
- 3 cups all-purpose flour
- 2 cups granulated sugar
- 1 teaspoon baking powder
- 3/4 teaspoon baking soda
- 1/2 teaspoon ground cinnamon
- 1/2 teaspoon salt
- 1/4 teaspoon ground nutmeg
- 1 cup unsweetened almond milk with 1 tablespoon lemon juice (substitute for 1 cup fat-free buttermilk)
- 3 large eggs
- 1/2 cup canola oil
- 1 tablespoon lemon zest (grated)
- 1/2 teaspoon pure vanilla extract
- 2 cups fresh blueberries

Instructions:
1. Preheat oven to 350°F (175°C). Spray a 10-inch Bundt pan with nonstick spray and dust with flour. Set aside.
2. In a large bowl, mix together the flour, sugar, baking powder, baking soda, cinnamon, salt, and nutmeg.
3. In a second bowl, whisk together the almond milk mixture, eggs, oil, lemon zest, and vanilla extract.
4. Add the wet almond milk mixture to the dry flour mixture and stir until just blended.
5. Gently fold in the fresh blueberries.
6. Pour the batter into the prepared Bundt pan.
7. Bake for 60-70 minutes, or until a toothpick inserted into the center comes out clean.
8. Let the cake cool in the pan for 15 minutes.
9. Carefully remove the cake from the pan and let it cool completely on a wire rack.

**Modified Recipe: Spaghetti Sauce With Meat**

**Ingredients:**
- 60 oz. tomato paste
- 290 oz. crushed tomatoes
- 105 oz. tomato soup (ensure it's shellfish-free and no cross-contamination)
- 2 large onions, diced
- 6 to 8 cloves garlic, diced
- 1 cup dry spaghetti sauce mix (check for shellfish-free certification)
- 15 lb. ground beef
- 4 to 6 Tbsp. Italian seasoning or to taste (ensure all ingredients are herbs and spices without additional shellfish-derived additives)
- Grated Parmesan cheese (check for shellfish contamination in processing)

**Directions:**
1. Brown ground beef in a large skillet over medium heat until fully cooked. Drain excess fat if necessary.
2. In a separate pan, sauté diced onions and garlic in a small amount of olive oil over medium heat until onions become translucent and garlic is fragrant.
3. Combine cooked onions and garlic with the ground beef and set aside.
4. In a large pot, mix together the tomato paste, crushed tomatoes, tomato soup, and dry spaghetti sauce mix. Add Italian seasoning and stir well.
5. Gradually add water to achieve the desired sauce consistency, stirring continuously.
6. Blend the ground beef, onions, and garlic mixture into the tomato sauce in the pot.

8. Serve hot over your choice of pasta, garnished with grated Parmesan cheese.

Evaluation of the recipe:

Case 114-Title: Chicken and Shallot Jam on Pain au Levain Recipe
Ingredients: ["2 (8-ounce) boneless, skinless chicken breasts", "1 medium yellow onion, quartered", "2 bay leaves", "10 whole black peppercorns", "2 teaspoons kosher salt", "2 tablespoons olive oil", "1 tablespoon unsalted butter", "1 1/2 pounds shallots, peeled, halved, and sliced 1/4-inch thick", "1/2 teaspoon kosher salt", "Freshly ground black pepper", "1/4 cup plus 2 tablespoons white wine-tarragon vinegar", "1/4 cup granulated sugar", "2 tablespoons coarsely chopped fresh tarragon leaves", "8 (1/2-inch thick) slices crusty bread, such as pain au levain"]
Directions: ["Place all the ingredients in a medium saucepan.", "Cover with cold water by 1 to 2 inches and bring to a simmer over medium-high heat; reduce heat to medium low and simmer gently until the chicken is completely cooked and no longer pink in the center, about 20 minutes.", "Remove the chicken from the poaching liquid to a cutting board and let cool to room temperature.", "Meanwhile, make the shallot-tarragon jam.", "Heat the oil and butter in a large frying pan over medium heat until the butter is foaming.", "Add the shallots, salt, and pepper and cook, stirring occasionally, until the shallots are softened and just beginning to brown, about 10 minutes.", "Stir in 1/4 cup of the vinegar and the sugar and cook, stirring occasionally, until the shallots are completely soft and caramelized and the jam is thick and syrupy, about 20 to 25 minutes.", "Remove the pan from heat and stir in remaining 2 tablespoons of vinegar.", "Let the jam cool for 20 minutes, then stir in the chopped tarragon.", "Slice the chicken into 1/4-inch thick pieces.", "Evenly divide the shallot jam on 1 side of 4 slices of the bread.", "Divide the chicken evenly among the sandwiches, placing it on top of the jam in an even layer.", "Close each sandwich and serve."]
Requirement: Lupin-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Recipe: Chicken and Shallot Jam on Pain au Levain**

**Ingredients:**
- 2 (8-ounce) boneless, skinless chicken breasts
- 1 medium yellow onion, quartered
- 2 bay leaves
- 10 whole black peppercorns
- 2 teaspoons kosher salt
- 2 tablespoons olive oil
- 1 tablespoon unsalted butter (ensure it is lupin-free or use a lupin-free butter alternative)
- 1 1/2 pounds shallots, peeled, halved, and sliced 1/4-inch thick
- 1/2 teaspoon kosher salt
- Freshly ground black pepper
- 1/4 cup plus 2 tablespoons white wine-tarragon vinegar
- 1/4 cup granulated sugar
- 2 tablespoons coarsely chopped fresh tarragon leaves
- 8 (1/2-inch thick) slices crusty bread, such as pain au levain

**Instructions:**
1. In a medium saucepan, place chicken breasts, quartered onion, bay leaves, black peppercorns, and 2 teaspoons kosher salt.
2. Cover ingredients with cold water by 1 to 2 inches.
3. Bring to a simmer over medium-high heat, then reduce heat to medium-low and simmer gently until the chicken is cooked through, about 20 minutes.
4. Remove the chicken from the poaching liquid and place on a cutting board to cool to room temperature.
5. While the chicken is cooling, prepare the shallot-tarragon jam. Heat the olive oil and lupin-free butter in a large frying pan over medium heat until butter is foaming.
6. Add the shallots, 1/2 teaspoon salt, and freshly ground black pepper. Cook, stirring occasionally, until the shallots are softened and just beginning to brown, about 10 minutes.
7. Stir in 1/4 cup of the vinegar and the sugar. Cook, stirring occasionally, until shallots are completely soft, caramelized, and the mixture is thick and syrupy, about 20 to 25 minutes.
8. Remove the pan from heat and stir in the remaining 2 tablespoons of vinegar. Allow to cool for 20 minutes, then stir in the chopped tarragon.
9. Slice the cooled chicken into 1/4-inch thick pieces.
10. Spread the shallot jam evenly on one side of 4 slices of the bread.
11. Divide the sliced chicken evenly among the sandwiches, placing it on top of the jam.
12. Close each sandwich with the remaining slices of bread and serve immediately.

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

While the modified recipe specifies the use of "lupin-free" butter or a lupin-free butter alternative, it does not address potential lupin cross-contamination in other ingredients, especially in the bread (pain au levain) or other processed ingredients like the vinegar and granulated sugar. When dealing with lupin allergy, stringent checks are necessary to ensure that all components, particularly those susceptible to cross-contamination during manufacturing processes, are certified lupin-free. Please verify that all ingredients have been properly certified to avoid potential risks.

Requirement: Gluten-free

The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Southern Bread Pudding (Gluten-Free):**

Ingredients:
- 2 cups almond milk (or any preferred plant-based milk)
- 4 eggs, beaten
- 1 tablespoon pure vanilla extract
- 1 cup raisins (optional)
- 4 cups gluten-free biscuit crumbs or gluten-free bread crumbs
- 2 tablespoons unsalted butter (or dairy-free alternative), melted
- Nutmeg to taste

Directions:
1. Preheat the oven to 350°F (175°C). Grease a baking dish with a small amount of melted butter or non-stick spray.
2. In a saucepan, mix almond milk, beaten eggs, and vanilla extract. Place over medium heat until the mixture is hot, but do not let it boil.
3. In a bowl, combine the gluten-free biscuit crumbs with the melted butter until well mixed. Line the bottom of the prepared baking dish with this crumb mixture.
4. Pour the hot milk and egg mixture evenly over the biscuit crumbs in the baking dish.
5. If using, sprinkle raisins evenly across the surface of the mixture.
6. Sprinkle nutmeg over the top to taste.
7. Place the baking dish in a larger pan filled with hot water to create a water bath.
8. Bake in the preheated oven for 45 minutes or until the top is golden and a knife inserted in the center comes out clean.
9. Allow to cool slightly before serving.

Case 117-Title: Tortilla Espanola (Potato Omelette)
Ingredients: ["2 pounds new potatoes scrubbed", "2 each onions yellow, sweet", "1 x olive oil, extra-virgin for frying", "4 cloves garlic chopped", "6 large eggs beaten", "1 x kosher salt", "1 x white pepper"]
Directions: ["Leaving the skins on, slice the new potatoes thinly.", "Peel, split, and slice onions.", "In a large saute pan, heat olive oil (the best you can afford).", "You need a good quarter inch in your pan.", "Saute potatoes and onions and garlic on a low flame until the potatoes are soft and the onions are translucent.", "Remove with a slotted spoon and place the potato mxture in a greased round cake pan, spring form pan, cast iron skillet or terra-cotta baking dish.", "If you use something small, make two.", "Season eggs and pour over potatoes.", "Bake 20 minutes at 350F (180C) F and then start testing.", "When the middle is set and the top slightly brown, it's done.", "Let set 5 minutes, run a knife around the outside and invert onto a round platter.", "Serve at room temperature."]
Requirement: Dairy-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Recipe: Dairy-Free Tortilla Espanola (Potato Omelette)**

Ingredients:
- 2 pounds new potatoes, scrubbed
- 2 yellow onions, sweet
- Olive oil, extra-virgin, for frying
- 4 cloves garlic, chopped
- 6 large eggs, beaten
- 1 teaspoon kosher salt
- 1/2 teaspoon white pepper

Directions:
1. Leaving the skins on, slice the new potatoes thinly.
2. Peel, split, and slice onions.
3. In a large sauté pan, heat extra-virgin olive oil (the best you can afford), ensuring there is a good quarter inch in your pan.
4. Sauté potatoes, onions, and garlic on a low flame until the potatoes are soft and the onions are translucent.
5. Remove with a slotted spoon and place the potato mixture in a greased round cake pan, springform pan, cast iron skillet, or terra-cotta baking dish.
6. If you use something small, make two.
7. Season the beaten eggs with kosher salt and white pepper, then pour over the potatoes.
8. Bake in a preheated oven at 350°F (180°C) for 20 minutes, then begin testing for doneness.
9. When the middle is set and the top is slightly brown, it's done.
10. Let set for 5 minutes, run a knife around the outside, and invert onto a round platter.
11. Serve at room temperature.

- 1 (16 oz.) bag frozen vegetables (broccoli, cauliflower, and carrots), thawed and drained

Case 119-Title: Baked Beans

Directions: ["Mix everything together and cook.", "You can cook on top of the stove with LOW HEAT and stir often.", "Or you can place in oven at 300 degrees and stir about every 1/2 hour.", "Cook beans until you have the thickness you desire.", "(I cook them about 2 - 2 1/2 hours, we like them thick.)"]
Requirement: Egg-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Recipe:**

Ingredients:
- 4 - 16 oz cans navy beans or cannellini beans (drained)
- 1 - 15 oz can kidney beans (drained)
- 1 - 15.5 oz can chili beans or canned pinto beans with 1 tsp chili powder
- 1 - 24 oz bottle tomato sauce (ensure allergen-free brand)
- 1/2 cup maple syrup
- 1/4 cup apple cider vinegar
- 3 cups brown sugar
- 1 large onion (diced) or 1 cup dried onions

4. Stir all ingredients together until well combined.

6. Place the dish in the preheated oven and bake for 2 to 2 1/2 hours, stirring every 30 minutes.
7. Continue baking until the beans reach the desired thickness.
8. Once cooked, remove from the oven and let cool slightly before serving.

Case 120-Title: Blue Cheese Pate Recipe
Ingredients: ["2 slc bacon", "1 x 8-oz package cream cheese, softened", "1 x 4 3/4-oz can liver spread", "1/2 c. crumbled blue cheese (2 ounces)", "2 Tbsp. dry sherry", "1/2 x or possibly an 8-oz can water chestnuts, liquid removed and minced (1/2 c.)", "2 Tbsp. finely minced onion", "2 Tbsp. minced pimiento-stuffed green olives parsley sprigs sliced pimiento-stuff green olives"]
Directions: ["In a small skillet cook the bacon till crisp; drain.", "Crumble bacon and set aside.", "In a small bowl beat together the softened cream cheese, the liver spread, the crumbled blue cheese, and the dry sherry till fluffy.", "Stir in the water chestnuts, the finely minced onion, the minced olives, and the crumbled bacon.", "Turn into one 3-c. or possibly three 1-c. bowls or possibly molds; cover and refrigeratetill hard.", "Unmold onto plate(s).", "Garnish with parsley sprigs and sliced olives.", "Directions: Store the pate in the refrigerator."]
Requirement: Celery-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Blue Cheese Pate Recipe**

Ingredients:
- 2 slices turkey bacon
- 1 x 8-oz package non-dairy cream cheese, softened
- 1 x 4 3/4-oz can chicken liver spread
- 1/2 cup crumbled blue cheese alternative (2 ounces, plant-based option)
- 2 Tbsp. dry sherry or apple cider vinegar for a non-alcoholic option
- 1/2 cup coarsely chopped jicama (instead of water chestnuts)
- 2 Tbsp. finely minced shallot
- 2 Tbsp. minced green olives without pimientos
- Parsley sprigs
- Sliced green olives without pimientos

Instructions:
1. In a small skillet, cook the turkey bacon until crisp; drain.
2. Crumble the bacon and set aside.
3. In a small bowl, beat together the softened non-dairy cream cheese, the chicken liver spread, the crumbled blue cheese alternative, and the dry sherry or apple cider vinegar until fluffy.
4. Stir in the chopped jicama, the finely minced shallot, the minced olives, and the crumbled turkey bacon.
5. Transfer into one 3-cup mold or three 1-cup molds; cover and refrigerate until firm.
6. Unmold onto a plate.
7. Garnish with parsley sprigs and sliced green olives without pimientos.
8. Store the pate in the refrigerator.

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

This modified recipe attempts to address the requirement of being celery-free, but there are a few points that raise potential concerns:

1. **Ingredient Safety Concerns**:
    - The modified recipe includes "a crumbled blue cheese alternative (plant-based option)". While it avoids celery, it’s crucial to ensure that this plant-based cheese substitute does not contain, or is not processed with celery or its derivatives, which is a common concern for cross-contamination in certain plant-based products.
    - The non-dairy cream cheese and chicken liver spread should also be checked for potential cross-contamination with celery during processing or if they include celery themselves. 

2. **Requirement Fulfillment**:
    - While the direct elimination of any specified celery ingredient is apparent, verification that all substituted ingredients are also certified celery-free and are processed in a celery-free environment is necessary to avoid cross-reactivity.

3. **Cross-Contamination and Cross-Reactivity Risk**:
    - If the ingredients are not explicitly stated to contain no traces of celery or are not certified as celery-free, there remains a potential risk for cross-contamination, especially if the person is highly sensitive.

Ensure all ingredients used are from trusted sources with confirmation from the manufacturer about the absence of celery.

Ingredients: ["1-1/4 pounds boneless pork loin chops, cut into strips", "1/4 teaspoon pepper", "1/8 teaspoon salt", "1 tablespoon canola oil", "1 can (11 ounces) mandarin oranges", "1-1/2 cups water", "1 package (6.2 ounces) fast-cooking long grain and wild rice mix", "1/4 cup thinly sliced green onions"]

Meanwhile, drain oranges, reserving juice; set oranges aside.", "Add the water, rice mix with contents of seasoning packet, onions and reserved juice to the skillet. Bring to a boil. Requirement: Dairy-free

**Modified Recipe: Mandarin Pork And Wild Rice (Dairy-Free)**

**Ingredients:**
- 1-1/4 pounds boneless pork loin chops, cut into strips
- 1/4 teaspoon pepper
- 1/8 teaspoon salt
- 1 tablespoon canola oil
- 1 can (11 ounces) mandarin oranges in juice
- 1-1/2 cups water
- 1 package (6.2 ounces) fast-cooking long grain and wild rice mix (check the label for dairy-free)
- 1/4 cup thinly sliced green onions

**Directions:**

4. Bring the mixture to a boil. Reduce heat; cover and simmer for 10-12 minutes or until the pork is no longer pink and the liquid is absorbed.
5. Stir in the mandarin oranges; heat through before serving.

Case 122-Title: Sophie's cold honey sesame meatball noodles
Ingredients: ["60 ml Sesame seeds", "28 grams soy sauce", "25 grams breadcrumbs", "1 egg", "120 ml milk", "2 tsp garlic powder", "20 ml Sesame seed oil", "1 tbsp honey", "500 grams turkey mince (pork would also work really well)", "4 portions of noodles", "1 cucumber", "4 tbsp soy sauce", "2 tsp ginger puree", "1 tsp salt", "4 tsp honey", "2 tbsp Sesame seeds", "1 tsp minced garlic"]
Directions: ["MEATBALLS: Combine milk and breadcrumbs and leave for 5 minutes.", "Turn the oven on to 180C.", "After 5 minutes, combine the rest of the meatball ingredients.", "It will create quite a wet mixture.", "Make meatballs - I made mine mini, using a half tablespoon sized measure.", "This created about 24 meatballs.", "Place on a pre greased baking tray and bake for 15 minutes.", "Once cooked, leave to chill in the fridge.", "NOODLES: Cook noodles as per instructions.", "While they cook, combine your wet ingredients and mix thoroughly.", "When your noodles are done, run under a tap to cool.", "Drizzle with sesame oil and toss.", "Chop your cucumber, and put in your wet mixture with your noodles.", "Add your sesame seeds.", "When your meatballs are cool, add, and enjoy!", "NB: can also be enjoyed hot - just add your cucumber at the last minute."]
Requirement: Dairy-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Recipe: Sophie's Cold Honey Sesame Meatball Noodles (Dairy-Free)**

**Ingredients:**
- 60 ml sesame seeds
- 28 grams soy sauce
- 25 grams breadcrumbs
- 1 flax egg (1 tbsp ground flaxseed mixed with 2.5 tbsp water)
- 120 ml unsweetened almond milk (or any other dairy-free milk)
- 2 tsp garlic powder
- 20 ml sesame seed oil
- 1 tbsp honey
- 500 grams turkey mince (pork would also work really well)
- 4 portions of noodles
- 1 cucumber
- 4 tbsp soy sauce
- 2 tsp ginger puree
- 1 tsp salt
- 4 tsp honey
- 2 tbsp sesame seeds
- 1 tsp minced garlic

**Directions:**

1. **MEATBALLS:**
   - Combine the almond milk and breadcrumbs and leave for 5 minutes.
   - Preheat the oven to 180°C.
   - After 5 minutes, combine the rest of the meatball ingredients, including the flax egg in place of the egg.
   - The mixture will be quite wet. Form mini meatballs, using a half tablespoon-sized measure. This should yield about 24 meatballs.
   - Place on a pre-greased baking tray and bake for 15 minutes.
   - Once cooked, leave to chill in the fridge.

2. **NOODLES:**
   - Cook noodles as per instructions.
   - While they cook, combine the soy sauce, ginger puree, salt, and honey to create the wet mixture and mix thoroughly.
   - When the noodles are done, rinse under cold water to cool.
   - Drizzle with sesame oil and toss to coat.
   - Chop the cucumber and combine with the noodles in the wet mixture.
   - Add the sesame seeds and toss to combine.

3. Once the meatballs are cool, add them to the noodle mixture and serve.
   
   - **Option to Enjoy Hot:** If preferred warm, add the cucumber just before serving.

Directions: ["Place all the ingredients in a blender and blend briefly. Can add water if onion is particularly strong.", "They can be just shaken in a jar for a less emulsified dressing. both ways are great. Lasts for a couple weeks in the fridge."]
Requirement: Dairy-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Catalina Salad Dressing Recipe**

Ingredients:
- 2/3 cup extra virgin olive oil
- 1/4 cup agave syrup (or your preferred sweetener)
- 1/4 cup lemon juice
- 1 tablespoon grated onion
- 1 teaspoon salt
- 1/2 teaspoon dried celery flakes
- 1/8 teaspoon black pepper, to taste
- 1/2 teaspoon ground mustard
- 1 teaspoon paprika

Directions:
1. Combine all ingredients in a blender and blend briefly until well mixed. If the flavor of the onion is too strong, a small amount of water can be added to dilute it slightly.
2. Alternatively, for a less emulsified dressing, place all ingredients in a jar, seal tightly, and shake until well combined.
3. Store in the refrigerator for up to two weeks. Shake well before each use.

- 2 bell peppers, chopped

- 1/2 cup sugar (reduce from 1 cup for better nutritional balance)
- 1/2 cup avocado oil or extra virgin olive oil
- 3/4 cup cider vinegar
- 1 tsp. gluten-free Worcestershire sauce
- 1 tsp. celery seed (avoid caraway seed for better allergen safety)

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Recipe: Poached Salmon With Dill Horseradish Sauce (Celery-Free)**

**Ingredients:**
- 2 cups white wine
- 2 cups vegetable stock (ensure celery-free) or water
- 2 onions, coarsely chopped
- 1 small bunch dill
- 5 sage leaves
- 3 bay leaves
- 2 lemons, quartered
- Kosher salt and cracked black pepper
- 2 pounds salmon filet
- 2 tablespoons finely chopped dill
- 2 tablespoons prepared horseradish
- 2 tablespoons lemon juice
- 1/4 cup sour cream
- 1/4 cup mayonnaise (ensure celery-free)
- Sliced chives, to garnish

**Directions:**
1. Bring a kettle of water to a boil, then remove from heat.
2. In a large skillet, heat white wine, celery-free vegetable stock (or water), onions, dill, sage leaves, and bay leaves, and bring to a simmer.
3. Add lemon quarters to the liquid, squeezing each one into the skillet before adding it. Simmer for an additional 15 minutes. Season to taste with salt and pepper.
4. Add the salmon, skin side down, to the simmering liquid. Using the hot water from the kettle, add additional water if necessary to cover the salmon.
5. Cook until the salmon is just cooked through, about 8 minutes. Remove from the liquid and let sit for 15 minutes.
6. In a small bowl, mix together dill, horseradish, lemon juice, sour cream, and celery-free mayonnaise. Season to taste with salt and pepper.
7. Divide the salmon between 4 plates. Top with the dill horseradish sauce and sprinkle with chives.
8. Serve with a light green salad and a light white wine.

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

Case 128-Title: Creamy Tarragon Asparagus Tart
Ingredients: ["1 prebaked Pie crust--see my recipe for processor pie crust or use your favorite", "1 1/2 cups plain nonfat Greek yogurt", "1/2 cup milk", "3 large eggs", "1 teaspoon salt", "1/2 teaspoon freshly ground pepper", "1 tablespoon each fresh tarragon and chives, minced", "zest of 1 lemon", "25 thin stalks asparagus, cut into 1 1/2 inch lengths"]
Directions: ["Preheat oven to 350F.", "In a mixing bowl, whisk together the yogurt, milk, eggs, seasonings, herbs, and zest, until well combined. Sprinkle the asparagus pieces into the bottom of the pie crust. Pour the egg/yogurt mixture over the asparagus, and place the pie tin on a baking sheet (to catch any spills in the oven).", "Bake for 35 minutes, or until lightly browned and puffy, and a knife inserted into the center comes out clean. There may seem to be a lot of liquid in the tart, but don't be alarmed. Let the tart sit for 10 minutes before cutting to serve and the liquid will magically be absorbed. This is also delicious served cold."]
Requirement: Corn-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Recipe: Creamy Tarragon Asparagus Tart (Corn-Free)**

Ingredients:
- 1 prebaked pie crust (ensure it's corn-free; consider a homemade crust using rice flour or almond flour)
- 1 1/2 cups plain nonfat Greek yogurt
- 1/2 cup whole milk (ensure it's corn-free)
- 3 large eggs
- 1 teaspoon sea salt
- 1/2 teaspoon freshly ground pepper
- 1 tablespoon each fresh tarragon and chives, minced
- Zest of 1 lemon
- 25 thin stalks asparagus, cut into 1 1/2 inch lengths

Directions:
1. Preheat oven to 350°F.
2. In a mixing bowl, whisk together the Greek yogurt, whole milk, eggs, sea salt, freshly ground pepper, minced tarragon, minced chives, and lemon zest until well combined.
3. Sprinkle the asparagus pieces into the bottom of the corn-free pie crust.
4. Pour the egg/yogurt mixture over the asparagus and place the pie tin on a baking sheet to catch any spills.
5. Bake for 35 minutes, or until the tart is lightly browned and puffy. Insert a knife into the center to ensure it comes out clean.
6. Let the tart sit for 10 minutes before cutting to serve. It can also be served cold.

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

1. Ingredient Safety: Ensure all pie crust ingredients are certified corn-free, including any additives or preservatives. Cross-contamination risks should be flagged when using commercially available products.

2. Whole Milk: Verify that the whole milk used is explicitly corn-free, as some dairy products may contain corn-derived additives or contamination from processing.

Always use certified corn-free products and check labels diligently to prevent accidental inclusion of corn derivatives.

Case 129-Title: Cold Salad
Ingredients: ["1/2 c. oil", "1/2 c. cider vinegar", "3/4 c. sugar", "1 tsp. salt", "1 tsp. pepper", "1 c. chopped celery", "1 c. chopped green peppers", "1 can Shoe Peg corn", "1 small can French-cut green beans", "1 small can peas", "2 bunches scallions"]
Directions: ["Mix oil, vinegar, sugar, salt and pepper over heat.", "Bring to boil until sugar is melted clear.", "Set aside.", "Mix all vegetables together in big bowl.", "Pour liquid over vegetables.", "Put in refrigerator for 1 hour or longer.", "Serve cold."]
Requirement: Dairy-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Cold Salad Recipe (Dairy-Free)**

**Ingredients:**
- 1/2 cup extra virgin olive oil
- 1/2 cup apple cider vinegar
- 3/4 cup honey or agave syrup (as a natural sweetener alternative to sugar)
- 1 teaspoon sea salt
- 1 teaspoon freshly ground black pepper
- 1 cup chopped celery
- 1 cup chopped green bell peppers
- 1 can (about 11 oz) Shoepeg corn, drained
- 1 small can (about 14.5 oz) French-cut green beans, drained
- 1 small can (about 15 oz) peas, drained
- 2 bunches scallions, thinly sliced

**Directions:**
1. In a saucepan, combine olive oil, apple cider vinegar, honey or agave syrup, sea salt, and black pepper.
2. Heat the mixture over medium until the honey or agave syrup is fully dissolved and the mixture is well combined.
3. Remove from heat and set aside to cool slightly.
4. In a large bowl, mix together the chopped celery, green bell peppers, Shoepeg corn, French-cut green beans, peas, and scallions.
5. Pour the warm dressing over the mixed vegetables and toss until well coated.
6. Cover the bowl and refrigerate for at least 1 hour or longer to allow the flavors to meld.
7. Serve cold and enjoy.

Case 130-Title: Shrimp Salad
Ingredients: ["2 (7 1/2 oz.) cans small shrimp", "1 medium can peas (early June)", "1 cucumber", "milk", "1 1/2 qt. cooked macaroni (any kind you like)", "1 small jar salad dressing (12 to 16 oz.)"]
Directions: ["Cook macaroni.", "In a large bowl, add shrimp, peas and cucumber (take inside seeds out of cucumber).", "Mix milk and salad dressing until creamy.", "Mix all ingredients together."]
Requirement: Soy-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Shrimp Salad Recipe**

Ingredients:
- 14 oz. fresh or frozen small shrimp (peeled, deveined)
- 1 cup frozen peas
- 1 medium cucumber (seeds removed, diced)
- 1 1/2 qt. cooked macaroni (gluten-free if needed)
- 1 cup plain Greek yogurt (dairy or non-dairy)
- 2 tbsp olive oil
- Salt and pepper to taste
- Lemon juice (from 1/2 lemon, optional)

Instructions:
1. Cook macaroni according to package instructions, then drain and set aside to cool.
2. If using frozen shrimp, thaw under cold running water, then pat dry. If using fresh, ensure they are cleaned and cooked.
3. In a small pot, blanch the peas by boiling for about 2-3 minutes, then drain and set aside to cool.
4. In a large mixing bowl, combine the shrimp, peas, and diced cucumber.
5. In a separate small bowl, mix the Greek yogurt with olive oil until smooth and creamy. Adjust thickness with additional olive oil if necessary.
6. Add the yogurt dressing to the shrimp mixture, season with salt, pepper, and lemon juice if desired, and mix thoroughly.
7. Add the cooled macaroni to the shrimp mixture and gently fold in until everything is well coated with the dressing.
8. Chill in the refrigerator for at least 30 minutes before serving. Serve cold.

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

- Edibility and Nutritional Sense: The modified recipe is edible and nutritionally coherent, replacing the salad dressing with Greek yogurt adds a nutritional balance.
- Ingredient Safety: It is important to ensure that the plain Greek yogurt used is soy-free, as some yogurt brands might add soy lecithin as a stabilizer or flavoring. Additionally, ensure that the frozen peas are not processed in a facility that handles soy to avoid cross-contamination.
- Requirement Fulfillment: The requirement is to be soy-free. Provided that Greek yogurt and frozen peas are verified to be soy-free, this requirement can be met.
- Cooking Steps: The steps are logical and feasible with the modified ingredients.

Ensure all packaged ingredients, especially Greek yogurt, are checked to be soy-free.

Case 131-Title: Vegetarian Breaded Zucchini Sticks
Ingredients: ["3 zucchini", "1 cup flour", "12 cup breadcrumbs", "1 12 cups water", "12 teaspoon salt", "1 teaspoon basil leaves", "1 pinch black pepper", "1 pinch garlic powder or 1 pinch hing", "oil (for frying)"]
Directions: ["Quarter zucchini lengthwise and cut each piece in half.", "In bowl combine flour, bread crumbs and spices.", "Add water and stir.", "Fill skillet 1/3 full w/ oil, then heat.", "Dip zucchini pieces in batter and then into hot oil; fry on all sides until tender and crisp.", "Serve hot."]
Requirement: Dairy-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Recipe: Vegetarian Breaded Zucchini Sticks (Dairy-Free)**

Ingredients:
- 3 zucchini
- 1 cup all-purpose flour
- 1/2 cup panko breadcrumbs (ensure dairy-free)
- 1 1/2 cups water
- 1/2 teaspoon salt
- 1 teaspoon dried basil leaves
- 1 pinch black pepper
- 1 pinch garlic powder
- Oil for frying (use avocado oil or any neutral high-heat oil, ensuring it's free from dairy contamination)

Instructions:
1. Quarter zucchini lengthwise and cut each piece in half to make sticks.
2. In a bowl, combine all-purpose flour, panko breadcrumbs, salt, basil leaves, black pepper, and garlic powder.
3. Gradually add water to the dry mixture, stirring to form a smooth batter.
4. Heat a skillet with oil (about 1/3 full) over medium heat until hot.
5. Dip each zucchini stick into the batter, ensuring it is well-coated, then carefully place it into the hot oil.
6. Fry the zucchini sticks on all sides until they are golden brown, tender, and crispy.
7. Remove from oil and place on a paper towel-lined plate to drain excess oil.
8. Serve hot.

Case 133-Title: Zucchini Bread
Ingredients: ["2 cups raw zucchini, shredded", "3 eggs", "1 34 cups sugar", "1 cup vegetable oil", "2 cups flour", "14 teaspoon baking powder", "2 teaspoons baking soda", "2 teaspoons cinnamon", "1 teaspoon salt", "2 teaspoons vanilla", "1 cup walnuts, chopped"]
Directions: ["Place zucchini in a strainer, press and squeeze with your hands to get the excess liquid out.", "Beat eggs, sugar, and oil together in a large bowl.", "Add flour, baking powder, baking soda, cinnamon, salt, vanilla, and walnuts.", "Mix together with a wooden spoon or spoonula.", "Add drained zucchini, mix well.", "For Loaf Pans: pour into 2 greased loaf pans.", "Bake 55 to 65 minutes at 350 degrees, ( For Muffins: bake at 350 degrees for 25 - 30 minutes ) or until a wooden tooth pick inserted in the center comes out clean."]
Requirement: Lupin-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Zucchini Bread Recipe**

Ingredients:
- 2 cups raw zucchini, shredded
- 3 large eggs
- 1 3/4 cups granulated sugar
- 1 cup coconut oil, melted (ensure it's not mixed with any unlabeled oils)
- 2 cups all-purpose flour
- 1/4 teaspoon baking powder
- 2 teaspoons baking soda
- 2 teaspoons ground cinnamon
- 1 teaspoon salt
- 2 teaspoons pure vanilla extract
- 1 cup walnuts, chopped

Directions:
1. Place zucchini in a strainer, press, and squeeze with your hands to get the excess liquid out.
2. Beat eggs, sugar, and melted coconut oil together in a large bowl.
3. Add flour, baking powder, baking soda, cinnamon, salt, vanilla extract, and walnuts.
4. Mix together with a wooden spoon or spoonula.
5. Add drained zucchini and mix well.
6. For loaf pans: Pour the batter into 2 greased loaf pans.
7. Bake in a preheated oven at 350 degrees Fahrenheit for 55 to 65 minutes, or until a wooden toothpick inserted in the center comes out clean.
8. For muffins: Pour batter into muffin tins lined with paper liners or greased.
9. Bake muffins at 350 degrees Fahrenheit for 25 to 30 minutes, or until the tops are golden and a toothpick inserted in the center comes out clean.

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

- **Ingredient Safety**: While the modified recipe substitutes vegetable oil with coconut oil, potentially avoiding any risks of lupin contamination, there is no explicit certification provided to ensure the coconut oil is free from cross-contamination with lupin. Given the lupin-free requirement, it's important to ensure all ingredients, including flour and coconut oil, are certified lupin-free.

To ensure safety, double-check all ingredients, especially processed ones like flour and oil, for certification that guarantees they are lupin-free.

Case 134-Title: Pumpkin Bread
Ingredients: ["3 cups sugar", "1 cup salad oil (canola)", "4 eggs, beaten", "1 (16 ounce) can solid pack pumpkin", "2/3 cup water", "3 1/2 cups all-purpose flour", "1/2 teaspoon clove", "2 teaspoons baking soda", "2 teaspoons salt", "1 teaspoon baking powder", "1 teaspoon nutmeg", "1 teaspoon allspice", "1 teaspoon cinnamon"]
Directions: ["Cream the sugar and oil together.", "Add eggs and pumpkin, mixing well.", "Mix together the dry ingredients.", "Add dry ingredients to pumpkin mixture alternately with water.", "Pour into 2 well greased and floured 9 x 5 inch loaf pans.", "Bake at 350 degrees for 1 1/2 hours or until tests done.", "Let stand 10 minutes, remove from pan to cool.", "Note: To test for doness, insert a toothpick off center and if it comes out clean the bread is done."]
Requirement: Sesame-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Pumpkin Bread (Sesame-Free)**

Ingredients:
- 3 cups sugar
- 1 cup avocado oil or grapeseed oil (avoid sesame oil contamination)
- 4 eggs, beaten
- 1 (16 ounce) can solid pack pumpkin
- 2/3 cup water
- 3 1/2 cups all-purpose flour
- 1/2 teaspoon clove
- 2 teaspoons baking soda
- 2 teaspoons salt
- 1 teaspoon baking powder
- 1 teaspoon nutmeg
- 1 teaspoon allspice
- 1 teaspoon cinnamon

Directions:
1. Preheat the oven to 350 degrees Fahrenheit. Grease and flour two 9 x 5 inch loaf pans.
2. In a large mixing bowl, cream the sugar and avocado oil together until well blended.
3. Add the beaten eggs and solid pack pumpkin to the sugar-oil mixture, mixing well until smooth.
4. In a separate bowl, mix together the all-purpose flour, clove, baking soda, salt, baking powder, nutmeg, allspice, and cinnamon.
5. Gradually add the dry ingredients to the pumpkin mixture, alternating with the water, starting and ending with the dry ingredients. Mix until just combined.
6. Pour the batter evenly into the prepared loaf pans.
7. Bake in the preheated oven for 1 1/2 hours, or until a toothpick inserted off-center comes out clean.
8. Let the bread stand for 10 minutes in the pans, then remove to a wire rack to cool completely.

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

- Ensure that the avocado oil or grapeseed oil used is explicitly labeled as sesame-free. While both oils are not derived from sesame, cross-contamination can occur in processing facilities. Check packaging or manufacturer details for a certified sesame-free designation.
- Verify that all other ingredients, especially the more processed items like the canned pumpkin, do not have any risk of sesame contamination. Ingredients like flour and spices should be sourced from facilities that do not process sesame to avoid cross-contact.
- Although the modified recipe avoids direct use of sesame, maintaining a fully sesame-free environment is crucial. Ensure all utensils, bakeware, and preparation surfaces are free from any sesame residues or contaminants.

- 1/2 teaspoon salt
- 1/8 teaspoon nutmeg

Directions:

Ingredients: ["2 teaspoons paprika", "1 teaspoon salt", "1 teaspoon onion powder", "1 teaspoon white pepper", "1 teaspoon cayenne pepper", "1 teaspoon dried thyme", "3/4 teaspoon garlic powder", "1/2 teaspoon pepper", "1 roasting chicken (6 to 7 pounds)", "1 large onion, cut into wedges"]

Requirement: Sulfite-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

Savory Rubbed Roast Chicken (Sulfite-Free)

Ingredients:
- 2 teaspoons sweet paprika
- 1 teaspoon salt
- 1 teaspoon onion powder
- 1 teaspoon ground white pepper
- 1 teaspoon cayenne pepper
- 1 teaspoon dried thyme
- 3/4 teaspoon garlic powder
- 1/2 teaspoon freshly ground black pepper
- 1 roasting chicken (6 to 7 pounds), check labeling for sulfite-free assurance
- 1 large fresh onion, cut into wedges

Directions:
1. Preheat oven to 350°F. In a small bowl, mix the first eight ingredients.
2. Pat chicken dry and place on a rack in a roasting pan, breast side up. Rub seasoning mixture over the outside and inside of the chicken. Place onion inside the cavity. Tuck wings under chicken; tie drumsticks together.
3. Roast 2 to 2-1/2 hours or until a thermometer inserted in the thickest part of the thigh reads 170°F-175°F. (Cover loosely with foil if chicken browns too quickly.) Remove chicken from oven; tent with foil. Let stand 15 minutes before carving.

Evaluation of the recipe:

Additionally, vigilance in ingredient sourcing and thorough label checking are advised to avoid cross-contamination risks.

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Recipe for Peanut Butter Fudge (Wheat-Free)**

**Ingredients:**
- 3 cups white granulated sugar
- 1 1/2 cups milk (can substitute with almond milk or any preferred non-dairy milk)
- Dash of salt
- 1/4 cup unsalted butter (ensure it's labeled gluten-free)
- 1 teaspoon pure vanilla extract (ensure it's labeled gluten-free)
- 1 cup creamy peanut butter (ensure it's labeled gluten-free)

**Directions:**
1. In a medium saucepan over medium heat, combine the sugar, milk, and a dash of salt, stirring until the sugar is dissolved.
2. Bring the mixture to a boil. Continue to cook without stirring until the mixture reaches a soft-ball stage (approximately 235°F on a candy thermometer).
3. Remove the saucepan from heat.
4. Add 1/4 cup unsalted butter and 1 teaspoon pure vanilla extract, stirring until the butter is melted and the mixture is smooth.
5. Allow the mixture to cool to around 135°F.
6. Add the 1 cup of creamy peanut butter to the mixture, stirring until well combined and the fudge starts to thicken.
7. Pour the mixture into a lightly buttered dish or a dish lined with parchment paper.
8. Let the fudge set at room temperature until firm before cutting into squares.

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

1. **Cross-Contamination Risk**: Ensure that each ingredient, particularly almond milk (if used), unsalted butter, vanilla extract, and peanut butter, is certified gluten-free. Cross-contamination can occur during manufacturing processes, so it's crucial to verify the labels or check for certification to ensure these ingredients are not contaminated with wheat.

2. **Ingredient Safety**: Almond milk is a potential tree nut allergen. If preparing for someone with a nut allergy, ensure an alternative non-dairy milk is used that does not pose a risk.

3. **Cooking Steps**: The steps are logical and feasible with the modified ingredients. However, ensure vigilance in temperature measurement while cooking, especially when reaching the soft-ball stage (approximately 235°F) to avoid any issues in fudge consistency.

- 1 tsp. sugar
- 1/2 tsp. baking soda (certified allergen-free)
- 1/4 tsp. salt
- 2 Tbs. certified allergen-free vegan margarine, cut into small pieces
- 1 6-oz. container certified allergen-free plain soy yogurt (or any certified allergen-free plant-based yogurt)
- Certified allergen-free soy whipped cream (or any certified allergen-free plant-based whipped cream)

Directions:
1. To make Filling: Combine strawberries, sugar, and lemon juice in a bowl. Set aside.
2. To make Shortcakes: Preheat oven to 450°F (232°C). Coat a baking sheet with cooking spray.
3. Whisk together certified allergen-free flour blend, baking powder, sugar, baking soda, and salt in a bowl.
4. Rub certified allergen-free vegan margarine into the flour mixture with fingertips until the mixture resembles cornmeal.
5. Stir in certified allergen-free plain soy yogurt until a soft dough forms.
6. Pat dough into a 1/2-inch-thick square on a floured work surface using the same certified allergen-free flour blend.
7. Cut 4 biscuits with a 2 1/2-inch round cutter. Place on the prepared baking sheet.
8. Make 4 more biscuits from dough scraps. Bake for 9 to 11 minutes, or until tops are golden.
9. Split biscuits, and set bottoms on plates.
10. Spoon 3 Tbs. of the strawberry filling over each.
11. Top with 3 Tbs. of certified allergen-free soy whipped cream.
12. Top with biscuit tops, remaining strawberries, and a swirl of certified allergen-free whipped cream.

Directions: ["Heat oven to 350F.", "In a medium saucepan, put raw cubed chicken (cut it up with a pair of scissors to make quick work of it).", "Just cover with water, add a lid to the pot and bring to boil on high heat.", "Reduce heat to medium-high and cook no more than 3-4 minutes after bringing to the boiling point.", "Drain chicken and reserve.", "Melt butter in microwave in a microwaveable bowl.", "Crush Ritz crackers coarsely in the sleeve (I guessed at the amount needed.just use a sleeve).", "Don't pulverize them to powder.", "You want to be able to still see 1/4 inch bits in there.", "Stir crushed crackers into the melted butter.", "In a seperate microwave safe bowl, heat the two cans of cream of chicken soup until hot.about 90 seconds.", "Stir well.", "If it's not hot, nuke one more minutes (watch out.the stuff explodes if you overdo it!", ").", "Stir cubed and cooked chicken with hot soup.", "If using, mix in Monterey Jack all except 2 tablespoons Put mixture in a casserole dish and top with the buttered crackers and the reserved 2 tbsp of cheese.", "Bake, uncovered about 20 minutes or until crackers are golden brown and crispy.", "If you are adding the cous couse, prepare the cous cous (takes 5 minutes for the cous cous) and add the prepared cous cous at the same time you stir together all the ingredients.", "Enjoy!"]
Requirement: Gluten-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Recipe: Tastes Too Good to Be That Simple Chicken Casserole (Gluten-Free)**

Ingredients:
- 2-4 chicken breasts, cubed
- 29 ounces gluten-free cream of chicken soup (ensure it's certified gluten-free)
- 17 gluten-free crackers (such as gluten-free buttery crackers, crushed)
- 1/2 cup butter or a gluten-free butter substitute, melted
- 1/2 cup Monterey Jack cheese (optional)
- 1 cup prepared gluten-free couscous or cooked quinoa

Directions:
1. Preheat the oven to 350°F (175°C).
2. In a medium saucepan, place raw cubed chicken and just cover with water. Add a lid to the pot and bring to a boil on high heat.
3. Reduce heat to medium-high and cook for no more than 3-4 minutes after reaching boiling point.
4. Drain the chicken and set aside.
5. Melt the butter or butter substitute in the microwave in a microwaveable bowl.
6. Crush the gluten-free crackers coarsely, maintaining small pieces about 1/4 inch in size.
7. Stir the crushed crackers into the melted butter.
8. In a separate microwave-safe bowl, heat the two cans of gluten-free cream of chicken soup until hot, about 90 seconds. Stir well.
9. Combine the cooked chicken with the hot soup. If using, mix in Monterey Jack cheese, saving 2 tablespoons for later.
10. Transfer the mixture to a casserole dish. Top it with the buttered cracker mixture and the reserved 2 tablespoons of cheese.
11. Bake, uncovered, for about 20 minutes or until the crackers are golden brown and crispy.
12. If you are adding gluten-free couscous or quinoa, prepare it according to package instructions and add when mixing all the ingredients together.
13. Enjoy!

Case 143-Title: Blackberry Cake
Ingredients: ["2/3 c. butter", "1 1/2 c. sugar", "2 eggs", "2 c. flour", "1 tsp. soda", "1/2 c. milk", "1 tsp. cinnamon", "1 tsp. nutmeg", "2 tsp. cocoa", "3 c. blackberries"]
Directions: ["Cream butter, sugar and eggs.", "Add flour alternately with milk.", "Add spices and cocoa.", "Fold in blackberries.", "Batter will be thick.", "Spoon batter into loaf pan.", "Bake at 350\u00b0 for 40 to 45 minutes."]
Requirement: Shellfish-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Blackberry Cake (Shellfish-Free)**

**Ingredients:**
- 2/3 cup unsalted butter
- 1 1/2 cups granulated sugar
- 2 large eggs
- 2 cups all-purpose flour
- 1 teaspoon baking soda
- 1/2 cup whole milk
- 1 teaspoon ground cinnamon
- 1 teaspoon ground nutmeg
- 2 teaspoons unsweetened cocoa powder
- 3 cups fresh blackberries

**Instructions:**

1. Preheat your oven to 350°F (175°C). Grease a loaf pan and set aside.
2. In a large mixing bowl, cream together the unsalted butter and granulated sugar until light and fluffy.
3. Add the eggs one at a time, beating well after each addition.
4. In a separate bowl, combine the all-purpose flour and baking soda.
5. Gradually add the flour mixture to the creamed mixture alternately with the milk, beginning and ending with the flour. Mix gently after each addition.
6. Stir in the ground cinnamon, ground nutmeg, and unsweetened cocoa powder until well distributed.
7. Carefully fold the fresh blackberries into the batter. The batter will be thick.
8. Spoon the batter evenly into the prepared loaf pan.
9. Bake in the preheated oven for 40 to 45 minutes or until a toothpick inserted into the center of the cake comes out clean.
10. Allow the cake to cool in the pan for a few minutes before transferring it to a wire rack to cool completely.

Requirement: Dairy-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Dish Name:** Mormors Dairy-Free Danish Crepes

**Ingredients:**
- 1 cup all-purpose flour
- 1 teaspoon salt
- 1 teaspoon baking powder
- 2 tablespoons icing sugar
- 2 large eggs
- 1 cup almond milk (or other plant-based milk)
- 1/2 teaspoon vanilla extract
- 1 tablespoon lemon juice
- 2 tablespoons icing sugar
- 1 tablespoon vegetable oil (for cooking)

**Directions:**
1. Sift the flour, salt, baking powder, and icing sugar together into a bowl and make a well in the center.
2. In a separate bowl, beat the eggs and add the almond milk, vanilla extract, and lemon juice.
3. Pour the beaten liquid mixture into the flour mixture.
4. Stir gently until just combined, ensuring not to over mix; it's fine if there are small lumps.
5. Heat a griddle or a non-stick skillet over medium heat and lightly coat with vegetable oil.
6. Pour a small ladle of the batter onto the hot griddle, allowing it to spread into a thin layer.
7. Cook until the edges are set and the bottom is lightly browned, then flip and cook the other side.
8. Fill each crepe with fresh fruit of choice and roll into tubes.
9. Optionally, sprinkle with fresh lemon juice and sift additional icing sugar over the rolled crepes before serving.

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

When serving this dish to someone who needs a dairy-free diet due to allergies, it's important to confirm that the almond milk used is certified nut-free if required, or to use an alternative plant-based milk that does not pose an allergy risk.

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Recipe: Gluten-Free Parmesan Corn Chowder**

**Ingredients:**
- 2 cups boiling water
- 1/2 cup carrots, sliced
- 1 1/2 teaspoons salt
- 1/4 cup dairy-free margarine (ensure it's certified gluten-free)
- 2 cups milk (or unsweetened almond milk for dairy-free)
- 1 (17 oz.) can creamed corn (ensure it's gluten-free)
- 2 cups diced potatoes
- 1/2 cup sliced celery

Case 152-Title: Home Done Pickled Beets
Ingredients: ["2 c. vinegar", "1 c. sugar", "1 1/2 c. water", "nutmeg", "allspice", "cloves", "cinnamon"]
Directions: ["Cook beets.", "Peel and pack in jars. Pour liquid over and seal."]
Requirement: Shellfish-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Recipe for Home Done Pickled Beets**

Ingredients:
- 2 cups apple cider vinegar
- 1 cup coconut sugar (or other preferred sugar alternative)
- 1 1/2 cups water
- 1/4 teaspoon ground nutmeg
- 1/4 teaspoon ground allspice
- 1/4 teaspoon ground cloves
- 1 cinnamon stick

Instructions:
1. Cook fresh beets until tender. Allow them to cool, then peel.
2. Slice the peeled beets and pack them tightly into sterilized jars.
3. In a saucepan, combine the apple cider vinegar, coconut sugar, water, ground nutmeg, ground allspice, ground cloves, and the cinnamon stick.
4. Bring the mixture to a boil, stirring until the sugar is dissolved. Let it simmer for about 5 minutes.
5. Pour the hot liquid over the beets in the jars, ensuring the beets are completely submerged.
6. Seal the jars with sterilized lids and process them in a boiling water bath for 10 minutes to ensure they are properly sealed.
7. Allow jars to cool at room temperature, then store them in a cool, dark place. Wait at least one week before opening for optimal flavor.

- 6 strips lasagna (ensure it is mustard-free)
- 1/2 cup chopped onion

- 1/4 cup all-purpose flour
- 2 cups chopped fresh or frozen vegetables (such as bell peppers, zucchini, broccoli)
- 1 cup milk (use lactose-free or plant-based milk like oat milk if needed)
- 1/3 cup lemon juice
- 1 1/2 cups shredded Mozzarella cheese

9. Bake the assembled dish in a preheated oven at 350°F (175°C) for 25-30 minutes, or until the cheese is bubbly and golden.
10. Allow to cool slightly before serving. Enjoy your mustard-free Tuna Pasta Bake!

Case 157-Title: Spanakopizza
Ingredients: ["1 pizza dough, refrigerated or from your favorite pizzeria", "1 tablespoon extra-virgin olive oil, 1 turn of the pan, plus some for drizzling", "1 teaspoon dried oregano, lightly crushed in the palm", "1 tablespoon butter", "1 pound ground chicken or turkey breast", "1/2 red onion, chopped", "2 cloves garlic, chopped", "1 tablespoon grill seasoning, a palm full (recommended: Montreal Steak Seasoning by McCormick)", "2 (10-ounce) boxes, frozen spinach, defrosted", "1 cup feta crumbles", "Salt and freshly ground black pepper", "2 cups shredded mozzarella cheese or shredded provolone", "2 jars roasted red peppers, drained", "1/4 cup (10 to 12) pitted kalamata olives", "1 cup arugula, coarsely chopped or shredded or 1/4 cup chopped flat-leaf parsley", "1/3 seedless cucumber, thinly sliced lengthwise", "Hot pepper rings or pepperoncini, optional"]
Directions: ["Heat oven to 425 degrees F.", "Stretch out your dough on to a pizza stone or into a pizza pan.", "Pierce the dough with a fork, drizzle the dough with a touch of extra-virgin olive oil and sprinkle it with oregano.", "Bake dough 10 minutes.", "While the pizza dough bakes, heat a tablespoon of extra-virgin olive oil (1 turn of the pan) in a large nonstick skillet over medium to medium-high heat.", "Add butter to the warm oil, then the chicken or turkey.", "Lightly brown the meat 3 to 4 minutes, then add the chopped red onion, garlic and grill seasoning and cook 5 minutes more.", "Wring the defrosted spinach dry by twisting it in a clean kitchen towel over your sink.", "Add it to the meat, separating it with your fingers.", "Add in feta crumbles.", "Once the pizza has cooked 10 minutes, remove dough and top evenly with meat and spinach mixture.", "Cover the pizza with shredded mozzarella or provolone, roasted peppers and olives.", "Bake pizza another 13 to 15 minutes until cheese is bubbly and crust is crisp.", "Remove pizza from oven, top with chopped parsley or arugula, cucumbers and hot peppers and serve."]
Requirement: Celery-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Recipe: Spanakopizza (Celery-Free Version)**

**Ingredients:**
- 1 pizza dough, refrigerated or from your favorite pizzeria
- 1 tablespoon extra-virgin olive oil, plus some for drizzling
- 1 teaspoon dried oregano, lightly crushed in the palm
- 1 tablespoon butter
- 1 pound ground chicken or turkey breast
- 1/2 red onion, chopped
- 2 cloves garlic, chopped
- 1 tablespoon homemade grill seasoning mix (see below)
- 2 (10-ounce) boxes, frozen spinach, defrosted
- 1 cup feta crumbles
- Salt and freshly ground black pepper to taste
- 2 cups shredded mozzarella cheese or shredded provolone
- 2 jars roasted red peppers, drained
- 1/4 cup (10 to 12) pitted kalamata olives
- 1 cup arugula, coarsely chopped or shredded, or 1/4 cup chopped flat-leaf parsley
- 1/3 seedless cucumber, thinly sliced lengthwise
- Hot pepper rings or pepperoncini, optional

**Homemade Grill Seasoning Mix:**  
- 1 teaspoon paprika
- 1 teaspoon ground black pepper
- 1 teaspoon onion powder
- 1 teaspoon garlic powder
- 1 teaspoon dried thyme
- 1/2 teaspoon ground coriander
- 1/2 teaspoon red pepper flakes (optional)

**Directions:**
1. Preheat the oven to 425 degrees F.
2. Stretch out your dough onto a pizza stone or into a pizza pan.
3. Pierce the dough with a fork, drizzle it with a touch of extra-virgin olive oil, and sprinkle it with oregano.
4. Bake the dough for 10 minutes.
5. While the pizza dough bakes, heat a tablespoon of extra-virgin olive oil in a large nonstick skillet over medium to medium-high heat.
6. Add butter to the warm oil, then add the chicken or turkey.
7. Lightly brown the meat for 3 to 4 minutes, then add the chopped red onion, garlic, and homemade grill seasoning. Cook for 5 more minutes.
8. Wring the defrosted spinach dry by twisting it in a clean kitchen towel over your sink.
9. Add the spinach to the meat, separating it with your fingers. Mix in the feta crumbles.
10. Once the pizza dough has cooked for 10 minutes, remove it and top evenly with the meat and spinach mixture.
11. Cover the pizza with shredded mozzarella or provolone, roasted peppers, and olives.
12. Bake the pizza for another 13 to 15 minutes until the cheese is bubbly and the crust is crisp.
13. Remove the pizza from the oven, and top with chopped parsley or arugula, cucumbers, and hot peppers as desired. Serve immediately.

Case 158-Title: Pumpkin Lasagna
Ingredients: ["1 kg pumpkin, in small cubes (Hokkaido, Butternut)", "5 garlic cloves, minced", "1 large red onion, chopped", "50 ml white wine", "250 g ricotta cheese", "2 tablespoons parsley, chopped", "3 tablespoons pine nuts", "16 -20 lasagna sheets (no precooking)", "50 g mozzarella cheese", "50 g mature cheese (Fontina, GruyA re, BergkA se)", "50 g parmesan cheese (grated)", "60 g butter", "60 g flour", "850 ml cold milk", "100 ml cream", "1 dash nutmeg", "12 teaspoon vegetable broth (powdered)", "1 tablespoon olive oil (or butter)", "salt and pepper"]
Directions: ["Toast pine nuts in a non stick pan until golden brown and fragrant.", "Transfer to a plate and let cool.", "Peel pumpkin if required, deseed and chop into rater small cubes.", "Heat oil or butter in a large skillet and add chopped red onion and minced garlic.", "Let fry a bit.", "Now it's time to add the pumpkin cubes.", "Stir and let fry for about 3 minutes.", "Add white wine and ricotta.", "Stir.", "Salt and pepper to taste.", "Let boil until pumpkin is tender (about 10-15minutes).", "Add chopped parsley and pine nuts.", "For the sauce bechamel melt 60g butter in a pot and add flour.", "Stir frequently (best with a wire whisk) and let flour \"roast\" for about 30 seconds.", "Add cold milk and cream and stir (It's important that the milk is cold otherwise flour chunks will form and spoil the sauce).", "Add vegetable broth granulate, nutmeg, salt and pepper and bring to a boil.", "Let sauce boil for a couple of minutes until thick and creamy.", "Butter a casserole and spread sauce bechamel evenly (about 1 generous scoop).", "Cover casserole with lasagna sheets (it takes usually 4-5 sheets per layer).", "Cover lasagna sheets with sauce bechamel.", "Add pumpkin-filling.", "Sprinkle layer with 1/3 of cheese mixture.", "Repeat \"layering steps\" excluding the cheese-sprinkling until pumpkin filling is used up.", "Last layer: lasagna sheets, sauce bechamel and the rest of the cheese.", "Cover casserole (aluminium foil) and let bake at 225C for 30 minutes, uncover and bake for about 15 minutes until golden brown.", "Let lasagna \"rest\" for about 15 minutes before serving.", "Enjoy!", "(Don't forget to open windows for ventilations' sake in case you're using \"alpine cheese\" (Bergkase :))."]
Requirement: Lupin-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Recipe: Pumpkin Lasagna**

Ingredients:
- 1 kg pumpkin, in small cubes (Hokkaido, Butternut)
- 5 garlic cloves, minced
- 1 large red onion, chopped
- 50 ml white wine
- 250 g ricotta cheese
- 2 tablespoons parsley, chopped
- 3 tablespoons pine nuts
- 16 - 20 lasagna sheets (ensure lupin-free brand)
- 50 g mozzarella cheese
- 50 g mature cheese (use a lupin-free alternative to Fontina, Gruyère, or Bergkäse)
- 50 g parmesan cheese (grated)
- 60 g butter
- 60 g flour
- 850 ml cold milk
- 100 ml cream
- 1 dash nutmeg
- 1/2 teaspoon vegetable broth (ensure it is lupin-free)
- 1 tablespoon olive oil (or butter)
- Salt and pepper

Instructions:
1. Toast pine nuts in a non-stick pan until golden brown and fragrant. Transfer to a plate and let cool.
2. Peel pumpkin if required, deseed, and chop into small cubes.
3. Heat olive oil or butter in a large skillet and add chopped red onion and minced garlic. Let fry a bit.
4. Add the pumpkin cubes. Stir and let fry for about 3 minutes.
5. Add white wine and ricotta. Stir. Salt and pepper to taste. Let boil until pumpkin is tender (about 10-15 minutes).
6. Add chopped parsley and cooled pine nuts.
7. For the béchamel sauce: melt 60 g butter in a pot and add flour. Stir frequently (best with a wire whisk) and let flour "roast" for about 30 seconds.
8. Add cold milk and cream; stir until smooth. Add vegetable broth granulate, nutmeg, salt, and pepper. Bring to a boil.
9. Let the sauce boil for a couple of minutes until thick and creamy.
10. Butter a casserole and spread a generous scoop of béchamel sauce evenly.
11. Cover the casserole with lasagna sheets.
12. Cover lasagna sheets with béchamel sauce.
13. Add pumpkin filling.
14. Sprinkle a layer with 1/3 of the cheese mixture (combine mozzarella, mature cheese, and parmesan).
15. Repeat layering steps, excluding cheese sprinkling, until pumpkin filling is used up.
16. For the last layer: lasagna sheets, béchamel sauce, and the rest of the cheese.
17. Cover the casserole with aluminum foil and bake at 225°C for 30 minutes.
18. Uncover and bake for about 15 minutes until golden brown.
19. Let lasagna rest for about 15 minutes before serving. Enjoy!

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

The modified recipe aims to accommodate a lupin-free requirement by specifying lupin-free options for lasagna sheets, mature cheese, and vegetable broth. However, the following points need attention to ensure complete safety:

1. **Ingredient Certification**: The recipe mentions using lupin-free alternatives for certain ingredients, but it is essential to confirm that each ingredient used in the modified recipe is explicitly certified lupin-free. This certification ensures there is no risk of cross-contamination, which is crucial for allergy safety.

2. **Cross-Contamination**: Be vigilant about cross-contamination risks in the kitchen, particularly if the kitchen also handles foods containing lupin. Ensure all cooking utensils, surfaces, and equipment are thoroughly cleaned and free from any traces of lupin.

Once these precautions are carefully managed, the modified recipe can be considered safe for someone with a lupin allergy.

**Turkey Tortilla Casserole – Wheat-Free Version**

- 3 cups chopped, cooked turkey or chicken
- 1 can gluten-free cream of chicken soup
- 8 oz. shredded Cheddar cheese
- 10 to 12 (6-inch) corn tortillas, torn into bite-size pieces (ensure they are labeled gluten-free)
- 1 (4 oz.) can diced green chilies, drained

**Modified Choc Chip Banana Cake Recipe**

**Ingredients:**

- **FOR THE CAKE:**
  - 1-3/4 cup All-Purpose Flour
  - 2/3 cup Cane Sugar
  - 2 teaspoons Baking Powder (ensure sulfite-free brand)
  - 1/2 teaspoon Baking Soda (ensure sulfite-free brand)
  - 1/4 teaspoon Sea Salt
  - 1 cup Mashed Bananas (2-3)
  - 1/3 cup Coconut Oil (melted)
  - 2 tablespoons Almond Milk (or any preferred non-dairy milk)
  - 2 whole Eggs
  - 1/4 cup Dark Chocolate Chips (check for sulfite-free variety)

- **FOR FROSTING:**
  - 1/2 cup Soft Cashew Cream Cheese (ensure sulfite-free variety)
  - 1/2 cup Cane Sugar
  - 1 teaspoon Pure Vanilla Extract
  - 1/2 cup Soft Unsalted Butter (or use a sulfite-free vegan butter)
  - 1 cup Organic Powdered Sugar (ensure sulfite-free brand)
  - 1/2 cup Brewed Sulfite-Free Decaf Coffee (optional; brewed fresh)

**Instructions:**

1. Preheat oven to 350°F. Grease an 8x4x2" loaf pan or similar-sized cake pan.

2. In a large mixer bowl, combine 1 cup of the flour, cane sugar, baking powder, baking soda, and sea salt.

3. Add mashed bananas, melted coconut oil, and almond milk. Beat on low speed until blended, then increase to high speed for 2 minutes.

4. Add eggs and remaining flour; beat until fully blended. Stir in the dark chocolate chips.

5. Pour the batter into the prepared pan. Bake for 55 to 60 minutes or until a toothpick inserted near the center comes out clean.

6. Cool in the pan for 10 minutes on a wire rack, then remove from the pan and cool thoroughly on the rack. Wrap in plastic wrap and store for better taste the next day.

7. For the icing, mix the cashew cream cheese, cane sugar, and vanilla together. Gradually add the soft unsalted butter and organic powdered sugar until smooth. 

8. Add brewed coffee one tablespoon at a time to achieve desired consistency and flavor, or omit the coffee if preferred.

9. Once the cake is completely cooled, frost as desired. Enjoy!

However, the cashew cream cheese and dark chocolate chips, although mentioned to be sulfite-free in variety, may still pose a cross-contamination risk if not certified as such. Especially with nuts like cashew, it's crucial that the product is explicitly labeled as sulfite-free and processed in a sulfite-free facility.

- **Requirement Fulfillment**: No prohibited ingredients (sulfites) have been listed; however, the potential risk due to cross-contamination or lack of explicit labeling for certain items like cashew cream cheese needs to be considered.

- **Cooking Steps**: The steps outlined in the modified recipe are logical and feasible, using appropriate methods for these alternative ingredients.

Case 162-Title: Macaroon Kiss Cookies
Ingredients: ["1/3 c. butter", "3/4 c. sugar", "2 tsp. almond extract", "1 1/4 c. flour", "1/4 tsp. salt", "1 (9 oz.) pkg. milk chocolate kisses", "1 (3 oz.) pkg. cream cheese", "1 egg yolk", "2 tsp. orange juice", "2 tsp. baking powder", "5 c. flaked coconut"]
Directions: ["Cream butter, softened cream cheese and sugar until light and fluffy.", "Add egg yolk, almond extract and orange juice.", "Beat well. Combine flour, baking powder and salt.", "Stir in 3 cups flaked coconut.", "Cover dough and chill about 1 hour.", "Shape dough into 1-inch balls.", "Roll balls in remaining coconut.", "Place on ungreased cookie sheet.", "Bake at 350\u00b0 for 10 to 12 minutes or until lightly browned on bottom.", "Remove from oven and press a chocolate kiss into center of each cookie.", "Allow to cool 1 minute.", "Carefully remove cookies from sheet and cool until chocolate kisses are firm. Makes 4 1/2 dozen."]
Requirement: Celery-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Macaroon Kiss Cookies Recipe (Celery-Free)**

Ingredients:
- 1/3 cup unsalted butter
- 3/4 cup granulated sugar
- 2 teaspoons almond extract
- 1 1/4 cups all-purpose flour
- 1/4 teaspoon salt
- 1 (9 oz.) package milk chocolate kisses
- 1 (3 oz.) package cream cheese
- 1 egg yolk
- 2 teaspoons fresh orange juice
- 2 teaspoons baking powder
- 5 cups flaked coconut

Instructions:
1. In a mixing bowl, cream together the unsalted butter, softened cream cheese, and granulated sugar until the mixture is light and fluffy.
2. Add the egg yolk, almond extract, and fresh orange juice to the creamed mixture. Beat well until fully combined.
3. In a separate bowl, combine the all-purpose flour, baking powder, and salt.
4. Gradually stir the dry ingredients into the wet mixture until well mixed. Then, fold in 3 cups of flaked coconut.
5. Cover the dough and chill it in the refrigerator for about 1 hour.
6. Once chilled, shape the dough into 1-inch balls.
7. Roll each dough ball in the remaining 2 cups of flaked coconut.
8. Place the coconut-covered balls on an ungreased cookie sheet, spacing them adequately.
9. Bake the cookies in a preheated oven at 350°F (175°C) for 10 to 12 minutes or until they are lightly browned on the bottom.
10. Remove the cookies from the oven and immediately press a milk chocolate kiss into the center of each cookie.
11. Allow the cookies to cool on the baking sheet for about 1 minute, then carefully transfer them to a cooling rack to cool completely until the chocolate kisses are firm.

This recipe yields approximately 4 1/2 dozen cookies.

Directions: ["In a 13 x 9-inch baking dish, mix together soy sauce, honey, fresh minced ginger, red pepper flakes and chopped fresh garlic.", "Add in the halved pork tenderloin and turn to coat.", "Cover with plastic wrap and refrigerate 3 or more hours, turning occasionally to coat with marinade.", "Meanwhile steam the broccoli until only crisp-tender; drain and set aside.", "After the pork has marinated, heat about 1 tablespoon of peanut oil in a skillet.", "Add in the pork and reserve ALL marinade.", "Cook the pork until deep brown, turning often (it should take about 10-12 minutes to cook pork).", "Cut into about 1/2-inch thick slices.", "Wipe the skillet clean.", "In a small bowl combine orange juice, vinegar, cornstarch and all the reserved marinade from the pork.", "Heat about 1 tablespoon peanut oil in the skillet.", "Add in broccoli and saute on high heat until brown (about 1 minutes).", "Add in the pork slices and orange juice mixture; stir until sauce boils, thickens slightly and coats the broccoli and pork (about 1 minute).", "Season with salt and pepper.", "Transfer to a bowl and serve."]
Requirement: Egg-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Ingredients:**
- 1/4 cup tamari (gluten-free soy sauce alternative)
- 1/4 cup maple syrup (or agave nectar for a less sweet version)
- 1 tablespoon minced fresh ginger
- 1/2 - 1 teaspoon crushed red pepper flakes
- 1 - 2 tablespoon chopped fresh garlic (optional)
- 1 pork tenderloin (cut in half lengthwise)
- 7 cups fresh large broccoli florets
- 2/3 cup fresh orange juice
- 2 teaspoons rice vinegar
- 2 teaspoons arrowroot powder (cornstarch alternative for thickening)
- 1 - 2 tablespoon toasted sesame oil (peanut oil alternative)
- Salt and pepper to taste

**Instructions:**
1. In a 13 x 9-inch baking dish, mix together tamari, maple syrup, fresh minced ginger, red pepper flakes, and chopped fresh garlic.
2. Add in the halved pork tenderloin and turn to coat.
3. Cover with plastic wrap and refrigerate for 3 or more hours, turning occasionally to coat with marinade.
4. Meanwhile, steam the broccoli until it is crisp-tender; drain and set aside.
5. After the pork has marinated, heat about 1 tablespoon of toasted sesame oil in a skillet.
6. Add the pork and reserve all the marinade.
7. Cook the pork until deep brown, turning often (about 10-12 minutes). Cut into about 1/2-inch thick slices.
8. Wipe the skillet clean.
9. In a small bowl, combine orange juice, rice vinegar, arrowroot powder, and all the reserved marinade from the pork.
10. Heat about 1 tablespoon of toasted sesame oil in the skillet.
11. Add the broccoli and sauté on high heat until brown (about 1 minute).
12. Add the pork slices and orange juice mixture; stir until the sauce boils, thickens slightly, and coats the broccoli and pork (about 1 minute).
13. Season with salt and pepper.
14. Transfer to a bowl and serve.

**Modified Cool Whip Pudding Cake Recipe**

**Ingredients:**
- 1 cup oat flour (or gluten-free graham cracker crumbs)

Evaluation of the recipe:

**Mincemeat Upside Down Cake (Corn-Free Version)**

**Ingredients:**

- 1/4 cup unsalted butter, melted
- 1/2 cup brown sugar, firmly packed
- 1 1/3 cups mincemeat
- 1/2 cup crushed pineapple, ensure it's canned in juice rather than corn syrup
- 1 1/2 cups all-purpose flour
- 1 cup granulated cane sugar
- 2 teaspoons baking powder (ensure it's corn-free)
- 1/2 teaspoon salt
- 3 large eggs
- 1/3 cup sunflower oil or extra light olive oil
- 1 1/3 cups milk or dairy-free milk
- 1 teaspoon vanilla extract

**Directions:**

1. Preheat oven to 350 degrees F.
2. Spread melted butter evenly over the bottom of a 9" square cake pan or a 10" round cake pan.
3. Sprinkle brown sugar evenly over the butter.
4. Combine mincemeat and pineapple, then spread this mixture evenly over the butter and brown sugar mixture.
5. In a large bowl, combine flour, granulated cane sugar, baking powder, and salt.
6. In a separate bowl, whisk together eggs, sunflower oil, milk, and vanilla extract.
7. Gradually add the wet ingredients to the dry ingredients, mixing until just combined to form the cake batter.
8. Pour the cake batter over the mincemeat and pineapple mixture in the pan.
9. Bake for 55-60 minutes, or until a toothpick inserted into the center comes out clean.
10. Remove from oven and immediately invert the pan over a serving platter, leaving the cake in the pan for several minutes before removing.
11. Serve warm or cold, optionally with a hard sauce or whipped cream.

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

- Ensure that canned crushed pineapple does not contain any traces of corn syrup or corn-derived preservatives, which could present cross-contamination risks.
  
- The baking powder must be certified corn-free, as conventional baking powders typically contain cornstarch.

Pay attention to the above points to ensure the modified recipe fulfills the corn-free requirement fully.

- 1 lb. ground lamb or hamburger
- 1 teaspoon garlic salt

- 1/2 cup Greek yogurt (ensure it's lupin-free)
- 1/2 cup fresh mint, chopped
- 6 tablespoons lemon juice, divided
- 1/2 red onion, chopped
- 2 medium Roma tomatoes, diced
- 1/2 cup chopped black olives (ensure no lupin contamination)

- 1/4 cup + 2 tablespoons olive oil

**Lupin-Free Hummus Recipe:**
- 1 16 oz. can chickpeas, drained (reserve liquid)
- 1 1/2 tablespoons tahini (ensure it's lupin-free)
- 2 cloves garlic, crushed
- 1/2 teaspoon salt
- 1/4 cup reserved chickpea liquid
- 2 tablespoons lemon juice
- 2 tablespoons olive oil

**Instructions:**
1. **Cook Ground Meat:**
   - In a skillet, brown the ground meat with garlic salt and Greek seasoning. Drain any excess fat and set aside.

2. **Make Lupin-Free Hummus:**
   - In a blender, combine the chickpeas, reserved chickpea liquid, tahini, garlic, salt, lemon juice, and olive oil. Blend until smooth. Add more reserved liquid if needed to achieve desired consistency.

3. **Make the Yogurt Sauce:**
   - In a blender, combine Greek yogurt, 1/4 cup olive oil, 4 oz. feta, mint, 3 tablespoons lemon juice, and a sprinkle of salt and pepper. Blend until smooth.

4. **Build the Dip:**
   - In a shallow 1 1/2 quart dish, spread the prepared hummus on the bottom.
   - Top with the cooked ground meat.
   - Pour the yogurt sauce over the meat.
   - Layer with the lettuce, diced tomatoes, chopped onion, olives, and the remaining 4 oz. feta cheese.

5. **Serve:**
   - Serve the dip at room temperature with certified lupin-free pita chips.

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

2. **Potential Cross-Contamination:**
   - The use of almond milk may pose a cross-reactive risk for individuals with lupin allergies, especially if they also have nut allergies. It is advisable to ensure there is no cross-contact in manufacturing facilities and consider oat milk or another suitable lactose-free, lupin-safe alternative if almond milk potentially poses a risk.

Please carefully check product labels and certifications to mitigate any potential allergen or contamination issues related to lupin.

Case 173-Title: Tri-Colored Mochi
Ingredients: ["1 lb Mochiko", "2 1/2 cup Sugar", "1 tsp Baking powder", "1 can Coconur milk", "3/4 cup Water", "1 tsp Vanilla"]
Directions: ["Preheat oven 350", "Divide batter into 3 equal parts.", "Use food coloring (3) to each part.", "Making each a different calor.", "Cover with foil when baking.", "Add first layer to greased pan.", "Bake 15mins.", "After 15 mins add second layer, bake for another 20 mins.", "Then add third layer and bake for remaining 30 mins."]
Requirement: Gluten-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Recipe: Tri-Colored Mochi (Gluten-Free)**

**Ingredients:**
- 1 lb Mochiko (Sweet Rice Flour) 
- 2 1/2 cups Sugar
- 1 tsp Gluten-free Baking Powder
- 1 can (13.5 oz) Coconut Milk
- 3/4 cup Water
- 1 tsp Gluten-free Vanilla Extract
- Food Coloring (Ensure gluten-free, use three different colors)

**Directions:**
1. Preheat oven to 350°F (175°C).
2. In a large mixing bowl, combine Mochiko, sugar, and gluten-free baking powder. Mix well.
3. Add coconut milk, water, and vanilla extract to the dry ingredients. Stir until the batter is smooth and well combined.
4. Divide the batter into three equal parts in separate bowls.
5. Add one color of food coloring to each bowl, mixing until the desired shade is achieved.
6. Grease a baking pan with a neutral oil like avocado or a non-stick spray (ensure it's gluten-free).
7. Pour the first colored batter layer into the greased pan and smooth it out evenly.
8. Cover the pan with foil and bake in the preheated oven for 15 minutes.
9. Carefully remove the foil, pour the second colored batter layer on top of the first, smooth it out, and cover with foil again. Bake for an additional 20 minutes.
10. Remove the foil, add the third colored batter layer, smooth it evenly in the pan, and cover once more. Bake for another 30 minutes.
11. Allow the mochi to cool completely before slicing and serving.

Case 174-Title: Milnot Cheese Cake
Ingredients: ["1 (3 oz.) pkg. lemon jello", "1 c. boiling water", "1 (8 oz.) pkg. cream cheese", "1/2 c. sugar", "1 tsp. vanilla", "1 tall can Milnot (13 oz.), whipped", "3 c. graham cracker crumbs", "1/2 c. butter, melted"]
Directions: ["Dissolve jello in boiling water.", "Chill until slightly thickened.", "Cream together cream cheese, sugar and vanilla.", "Add jello; blend well.", "Fold in stiffly whipped Milnot.", "(Can be done with electric mixer.)", "Mix graham cracker crumbs and melted butter together.", "Put 2/3 of mixture on bottom and sides of a 9 x 13 x 2-inch pan.", "Add filling; sprinkle with remaining crumbs.", "Cut into squares; serve plain or garnished with fruit.", "Chill several hours or overnight.", "Serves 12 to 16."]
Requirement: Gluten-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Recipe for Gluten-Free Milnot Cheese Cake**

Ingredients:
- 1 (3 oz.) pkg. lemon-flavored gelatin (ensure it's gluten-free)
- 1 cup boiling water
- 1 (8 oz.) pkg. cream cheese
- 1/2 cup sugar
- 1 tsp. pure vanilla extract
- 1 tall can Milnot (13 oz.), whipped (or substitute with whipped coconut cream for a non-dairy option)
- 3 cups gluten-free graham cracker crumbs
- 1/2 cup melted butter (ensure gluten-free certified)

Instructions:
1. Dissolve the lemon gelatin in boiling water.
2. Chill the mixture until it is slightly thickened.
3. In a separate bowl, cream together the cream cheese, sugar, and vanilla extract until smooth.
4. Add the thickened gelatin mixture to the cream cheese mixture and blend well.
5. Fold in the stiffly whipped Milnot or whipped coconut cream, using an electric mixer if desired.
6. In another bowl, mix the gluten-free graham cracker crumbs with the melted butter until well combined.
7. Press 2/3 of the crumb mixture onto the bottom and sides of a 9 x 13 x 2-inch pan to form the crust.
8. Pour the filling over the crust and spread evenly.
9. Sprinkle the remaining crumb mixture on top as a garnish.
10. Cut into squares and serve plain or garnished with fresh fruit.
11. Chill in the refrigerator for several hours or overnight before serving.

Serves 12 to 16.

Case 175-Title: Spinach Dip With Homemade Pita Chips
Ingredients: ["4 -6 large pita breads", "1/2 teaspoon salt", "3 tablespoons olive oil", "4 ounces lipton dry vegetable soup mix", "8 ounces light sour cream", "1 cup light mayonnaise", "10 ounces frozen chopped spinach, thawed and squeezed dry", "8 ounces water chestnuts (optional)"]
Directions: ["To make the pita chips, split the pita breads in half and cut into 4 triangled shape pieces.", "Oil a large baking sheet with the olive oil and line the pita slices in even rows.
