The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Spinach Dip With Homemade Pita Chips**

**Ingredients:**
- 4-6 large pita breads
- 1/2 teaspoon salt
- 3 tablespoons extra-virgin olive oil
- 1 teaspoon dried onion flakes
- 1 teaspoon dried parsley
- 1 teaspoon garlic powder
- 8 ounces light sour cream
- 1 cup light mayonnaise
- 10 ounces frozen chopped spinach, thawed and squeezed dry
- 8 ounces water chestnuts (optional)

**Directions:**
1. Preheat your oven to 375°F (190°C).
2. To make the pita chips, split the pita breads in half and cut each half into 4 triangle-shaped pieces.
3. Oil a large baking sheet with the extra-virgin olive oil and arrange the pita slices in even rows. Sprinkle them with salt. For extra flavor, you may add some black pepper.
4. Bake the pita slices for about 10-12 minutes until they are toasted to a golden brown.
5. In a medium-sized bowl, mix together the dried onion flakes, dried parsley, and garlic powder.
6. Add the light sour cream and light mayonnaise to the bowl and stir well until the ingredients are fully combined.
7. Add the drained spinach and the optional water chestnuts to the mixture and stir well.
8. Chill the dip for at least 2 hours before serving.

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

However, the caution here lies in the assumption that the vegetable soup mix contains celery. Since that was not explicitly mentioned in the original, and the new ingredients do not include a celery or celery-derived component, the modification could be around 90% safe. The remaining caution lies in cross-contamination risks associated with the manufacturing process of dried herbs and spices. It's crucial to verify that the dried onion flakes, dried parsley, and garlic powder used are certified celery-free and do not pose a risk of cross-contamination.

Case 176-Title: Spicy Soy-Glazed Short Ribs
Ingredients: ["3 1/2 pounds beef short ribs", "2 bunches scallions, trimmed and thinly sliced on the diagonal", "1 clove garlic, minced", "1 1-inch piece fresh ginger, peeled and minced", "1/3 cup soy sauce", "1/4 cup rice vinegar", "1/4 cup molasses", "1/4 cup brown sugar", "1/4 cup chili-garlic sauce (see Note)", "1/4 cup plum or hoisin sauce (optional)", "Juice of 2 limes", "1 tablespoon toasted-sesame oil", "1 teaspoon cayenne pepper", "1/2 teaspoon freshly ground black pepper", "2 tablespoons sesame seeds"]
Directions: ["Trim any excess fat or sinew off the ribs.", "In a heavy skillet over medium-high heat, brown half of the ribs well on all sides, about 8 minutes total, then remove the ribs to a 4-quart slow cooker (they will fit better in an oval cooker); repeat with the remaining ribs.", "Pour 1/2 cup water into the skillet and scrape up all the browned bits in the bottom of the pan.", "Pour the liquid over the ribs in the cooker.", "In a medium bowl, combine half of the scallions and all the remaining ingredients except the sesame seeds, stirring until the brown sugar is dissolved.", "Pour the mixture over the ribs.", "Cook, covered, on the low setting for 4 hours, or until the meat is very tender and almost falling off the bones.", "In a small skillet over medium-high heat, toast the sesame seeds, shaking the skillet and stirring constantly, until they just begin to color.", "Transfer to a small bowl and set aside.", "Remove the ribs from the sauce and place on a large serving platter or on individual plates.", "Spoon a little of the sauce over the ribs and sprinkle with the sesame seeds and the remaining scallions.", "Serve."]
Requirement: Peanut-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Dish Name:** Spicy Soy-Glazed Short Ribs (Peanut-Free Version)

**Modified Recipe:**

Ingredients:
- 3 1/2 pounds beef short ribs
- 2 bunches scallions, trimmed and thinly sliced on the diagonal
- 1 clove garlic, minced
- 1 1-inch piece fresh ginger, peeled and minced
- 1/3 cup soy sauce (ensure it's peanut-free by checking the label)
- 1/4 cup rice vinegar
- 1/4 cup molasses
- 1/4 cup brown sugar
- 1/4 cup chili-garlic sauce (verify peanut-free)
- 1/4 cup plum sauce (optional, verify peanut-free) or substitute with additional soy sauce for reduced sweetness
- Juice of 2 limes
- 1 tablespoon toasted-sesame oil (confirm it's peanut-free, use a brand-specific version if necessary)
- 1 teaspoon cayenne pepper
- 1/2 teaspoon freshly ground black pepper
- 2 tablespoons sesame seeds (ensure not processed in a facility with peanuts)

Instructions:
1. Trim any excess fat or sinew off the ribs.
2. In a heavy skillet over medium-high heat, brown half of the ribs well on all sides, about 8 minutes total, then remove the ribs to a 4-quart slow cooker; repeat with the remaining ribs.
3. Pour 1/2 cup water into the skillet and scrape up all the browned bits in the bottom of the pan.
4. Pour the liquid over the ribs in the cooker.
5. In a medium bowl, combine half of the scallions and all the remaining ingredients except the sesame seeds, stirring until the brown sugar is dissolved.
6. Pour the mixture over the ribs.
7. Cook, covered, on the low setting for 4 hours, or until the meat is very tender and almost falling off the bones.
8. In a small skillet over medium-high heat, toast the sesame seeds, shaking the skillet and stirring constantly, until they just begin to color.
9. Transfer to a small bowl and set aside.
10. Remove the ribs from the sauce and place on a large serving platter or on individual plates.
11. Spoon a little of the sauce over the ribs and sprinkle with the sesame seeds and the remaining scallions.
12. Serve.

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

- Ensure all ingredients, particularly soy sauce, chili-garlic sauce, plum sauce, toasted-sesame oil, and sesame seeds, are certified peanut-free and not processed in a facility handling peanuts to avoid cross-contamination risks.
- Verify that substitute ingredients are certified allergen-free according to standardized testing to prevent any cross-reactivity issues.

Case 178-Title: 7 Minute Frosting
Ingredients: ["1 12 cups sugar", "14 teaspoon cream of tartar", "18 teaspoon salt", "13 cup water", "2 egg whites", "1 12 teaspoons pure vanilla extract"]
Directions: ["Place sugar, cream of tartar, salt, water, and egg whites in the top of a double boiler.", "Beat with a handheld electric mixer for 1 minute.", "Place pan over boiling water, being sure that boiling water does not touch the bottom of the top pan.", "(If this happens, it could cause your frosting to become grainy).", "Beat constantly on high speed with electric mixer for 7 minutes.", "Beat in vanilla.", "Don't let it stand too long, use immediately."]
Requirement: Dairy-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Recipe for Dairy-Free 7 Minute Frosting**

Ingredients:
- 1 1/2 cups granulated sugar
- 1/4 teaspoon cream of tartar
- 1/8 teaspoon salt
- 1/3 cup water
- 2 large egg whites
- 1 1/2 teaspoons pure vanilla extract

Directions:
1. Place sugar, cream of tartar, salt, water, and egg whites in the top of a double boiler.
2. Beat with a handheld electric mixer for 1 minute.
3. Place the pan over boiling water, being sure that boiling water does not touch the bottom of the top pan.
4. Beat constantly on high speed with electric mixer for 7 minutes.
5. Remove from heat and beat in vanilla.
6. Use immediately, as the frosting is best not left to stand too long.

Case 179-Title: Pesto Chicken Primavera
Ingredients: ["1 lb angel hair pasta", "1 (7 ounce) container refrigerated sun-dried tomato pesto, divided", "1 lb boneless chicken breast, cut into strips", "2 tablespoons olive oil", "1 red bell pepper, seeded and sliced thin", "1 orange bell pepper, seeded and sliced thin", "1 small red onion, peeled and chopped", "1 zucchini, quartered and sliced"]
Directions: ["Cook the pasta according to box directions. Toss the cooked pasta with 3 tablespoons of pesto sauce, put on platter and cover to keep warm.", "Salt and pepper the chicken strips, heat the olive oil over medium high heat and cook the chicken for five minutes in the hot oil; remove chicken set aside.", "In the same pan, cook the peppers and onions for 8 minutes, add the zucchini and cook 8 minutes more. Return the chicken to skillet and top the pasta with the mixture and remaining pesto; toss."]
Requirement: Corn-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Recipe: Pesto Chicken Primavera (Corn-Free)**

Ingredients:
- 1 lb gluten-free angel hair pasta (ensure it is corn-free)
- 1 cup homemade sun-dried tomato pesto (see recipe below)
- 1 lb boneless chicken breast, cut into strips
- 2 tablespoons olive oil (extra virgin)
- 1 red bell pepper, seeded and sliced thin
- 1 orange bell pepper, seeded and sliced thin
- 1 small red onion, peeled and chopped
- 1 zucchini, quartered and sliced
- Salt and pepper to taste

Homemade Sun-Dried Tomato Pesto:
- 1 cup oil-packed sun-dried tomatoes, drained
- 1/4 cup pine nuts
- 1/4 cup grated Parmesan cheese
- 2 cloves garlic
- 1/2 cup fresh basil leaves
- 1/4 cup extra virgin olive oil
- Salt to taste

Instructions:
1. Prepare the pesto: In a food processor, combine sun-dried tomatoes, pine nuts, Parmesan cheese, garlic, and basil leaves. Pulse until finely chopped. With the machine running, slowly add olive oil until the mixture is smooth and well combined. Season with salt as desired.

2. Cook the pasta according to package directions. Once cooked, drain and toss the pasta with 3 tablespoons of the homemade pesto. Place the pasta on a platter and cover to keep warm.

3. Season the chicken strips with salt and pepper. Heat olive oil in a large skillet over medium-high heat. Cook the chicken for about 5 minutes, or until fully cooked. Remove the chicken from the skillet and set aside.

4. In the same skillet, add the red and orange bell peppers and red onion. Cook for about 8 minutes, stirring occasionally. Then, add the zucchini and continue to cook for an additional 8 minutes, or until all vegetables are tender.

5. Return the chicken strips to the skillet with the vegetables, and stir to combine.

6. Top the pasta with the chicken and vegetable mixture. Drizzle the remaining pesto over the entire dish and toss gently to combine.

7. Serve warm, adjusting seasoning with additional salt and pepper if desired.

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

- **Edibility and Nutritional Sense:** The modified pesto sauce uses fresh and commonly accepted ingredients that ensure the nutritional value and taste of the original dish are maintained. Thus, the nutritional sense of the dish is consistent.

- **Ingredient Safety:** The modified recipe does not explicitly assure cross-contamination safety for the pasta, which should be ensured to be certified as corn-free apart from being gluten-free. Additionally, care should be taken that all ingredients used in creating the homemade pesto do not contain corn derivatives or contaminants, especially the Parmesan cheese and oil-packed sun-dried tomatoes, which can sometimes include corn-derived additives.

- **Requirement Fulfillment:** While the primary requirement to make the dish corn-free appears to be addressed by selecting a gluten-free pasta variant that specifies corn-free, often gluten-free products may contain traces of corn. Explicit certification for all components, particularly processed ones, should be sought after.

- **Cooking Steps:** The steps of preparation and cooking remain logical and feasible with the substitute ingredients in the modification.

The cautionary points primarily deal with verification and certification of corn-free status for certain ingredients to prevent any risk of inadvertent exposure.

  - 2 green shallots, ends trimmed, thinly sliced diagonally

**Method:**

1. Combine the water, stock cube, coconut aminos, lemon grass, lime leaves, ginger, chili, coriander roots, and garlic in a large saucepan. Bring to the boil over medium-high heat.
2. Gently simmer, covered, for 5-10 minutes or until fragrant and reduced slightly.
3. Remove from heat. Strain through a fine sieve into a clean large saucepan. Discard solids.
4. Meanwhile, combine the chicken, garlic, sliced green shallots, and lemon rind in a bowl. Soften the rice paper wrappers one at a time in warm water. Place 1 heaped teaspoonful of chicken mixture in the center of each wrapper. Wrap up each wonton as desired.
5. Bring the soup back to a simmer over medium heat. Add the wontons and asparagus and simmer, covered, stirring occasionally, for 4 minutes or until wontons are cooked.
6. Remove from heat. Stir in coriander and green shallot.
7. Divide wontons and soup among serving bowls. Serve immediately.

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

- **Requirement Fulfillment:** While the modified recipe aims to be soy-free by replacing soy sauce with coconut aminos and using rice paper wrappers, it assumes that these substitutes are certified soy-free. Without explicit certification, there remains a potential risk of soy contamination, especially for individuals with severe soy allergies. 

- **Ingredient Safety:** Verify that the vegetable stock cube and rice paper wrappers are explicitly labeled as soy-free to prevent cross-contamination or hidden soy derivatives.

The modified recipe seems to comply with the soy-free requirement, but it is essential to confirm that each substituted ingredient holds a soy-free certification to ensure safety, especially in the presence of severe allergies.

- 2 ripe bananas, sliced

**Instructions:**

- 1 dill pickle, quartered lengthwise

- 4 teaspoons unsalted butter, softened

**Directions:**

Case 187-Title: Vanilla Butter Rollouts
Ingredients: ["1-1/2 cups butter, softened", "1-1/2 cups sugar", "1 tablespoon vanilla extract", "2 large eggs", "4 cups all-purpose flour", "1 teaspoon baking soda", "1 teaspoon cream of tartar", "1 teaspoon salt", "6 tablespoons butter, softened", "3 cups confectioners' sugar", "1 tablespoon clear or regular vanilla extract", "3 to 4 tablespoons 2% milk", "Paste food coloring, optional", "Assorted decorations, optional"]
Directions: ["Cream butter and sugar until light and fluffy. Beat in vanilla and eggs, one at a time. Whisk together flour, baking soda, cream of tartar and salt; gradually beat into creamed mixture. Divide dough in half. Shape each into a disk; cover. Refrigerate 30 minutes or until firm enough to roll.", "Preheat oven to 350\u00b0. On a lightly floured surface, roll each portion to 1/4-in. thickness. Cut with floured 2-1/2- to 3-in. cookie cutters. Place 2 in. apart on ungreased", ".", "Bake until golden brown, 8-10 minutes. If desired, tint with food coloring. Spread or pipe onto cookies; decorate as desired."]
Requirement: Dairy-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Recipe for Dairy-Free Vanilla Rollouts**

Ingredients:  
- 1-1/2 cups dairy-free butter substitute (such as Earth Balance or coconut oil), softened  
- 1-1/2 cups sugar  
- 1 tablespoon vanilla extract  
- 2 large eggs  
- 4 cups all-purpose flour  
- 1 teaspoon baking soda  
- 1 teaspoon cream of tartar  
- 1 teaspoon salt  
- 6 tablespoons dairy-free butter substitute, softened  
- 3 cups confectioners' sugar  
- 1 tablespoon clear or regular vanilla extract  
- 3 to 4 tablespoons unsweetened almond milk (or any preferred plant-based milk)  
- Paste food coloring, optional  
- Assorted decorations, optional  

Directions:  

1. Cream together the dairy-free butter substitute and sugar until light and fluffy. Beat in the vanilla and eggs, one at a time.  
2. In a separate bowl, whisk together the flour, baking soda, cream of tartar, and salt. Gradually beat this dry mixture into the creamed mixture until fully incorporated.  
3. Divide the dough in half, shape each half into a disk, cover tightly, and refrigerate for 30 minutes or until firm enough to roll.  
4. Preheat the oven to 350°F (175°C). On a lightly floured surface, roll each portion to a 1/4-inch thickness. Use floured 2-1/2 to 3-inch cookie cutters to cut out shapes. Place the cookies 2 inches apart on ungreased baking sheets.  
5. Bake the cookies until they are golden brown, about 8-10 minutes. Remove from the pans and transfer to wire racks to cool completely.  
6. For the frosting, beat together the dairy-free butter substitute, confectioners' sugar, vanilla, and enough almond milk to reach the desired consistency. If desired, tint with food coloring. Spread or pipe the frosting onto the cooled cookies and decorate as desired.

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

- While the modified recipe attempts to replace dairy products with dairy-free alternatives, it uses almond milk as a substitute. Almonds are tree nuts, and individuals with dairy allergies are sometimes advised to be cautious of potential cross-reactivity or additional tree nut allergies. Ensure that the person following this recipe has no almond or other tree nut allergies.

- Additionally, confirm that the chosen dairy-free butter substitute is explicitly certified dairy-free to avoid cross-contamination risks. While "Earth Balance" is generally considered a reliable brand, always verify certification as manufacturing processes may vary.

Ensure these potential risks are considered for those with specific allergies.

Case 188-Title: Grammy'S Spaghetti Bake 
Ingredients: ["1 lb ground beef", "1 cup chopped onion", "1 cup chopped green pepper", "2 clove garlic, minced", "1 28oz can crushed tomatoes", "1 15oz can tomato sauce", "1 4oz can mushrooms, drained", "2 tsp sugar", "1 1/2 tsp oregano, crushed", "1 tsp salt", "1 tsp basil", "8oz spaghetti, broken,cooked, drained", "2 cups shredded Italion blend cheese", "1/3 cup grated parmesan"]
Directions: ["In Dutch oven cook ground beef, chopped onion, chopped green pepper and minced garlic until beef is browned and both onion and green pepper are tender, drain.", "", "Stir in undrained tomatoes, tomato sauce, mushrooms, sugar, oregano, salt and basil. Bring meat mixture to boil, boil gently, uncovered 20-25 minutes, stir occasionally.", "", "Remove meat sauce from heat, stir in drained spaghetti. Place half of spaghetti-meat sauce in 13x9x2 baking dish. Sprinkle with shredded mozzarella. Top with remaining spaghetti meat sauce. Sprinkle with grated parmesan cheese. Requirement: Corn-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Recipe for Grammy's Spaghetti Bake (Corn-Free)**

**Ingredients:**
- 1 lb ground beef
- 1 cup chopped onion
- 1 cup chopped green pepper
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 28oz can crushed tomatoes (ensure no corn-derived additives)
- 1 15oz can tomato sauce (ensure no corn-derived additives)
- 1 4oz can mushrooms, drained
- 2 tsp sugar
- 1 1/2 tsp oregano, crushed
- 1 tsp salt
- 1 tsp basil
- 8oz spaghetti, broken, cooked, drained (ensure corn-free)
- 2 cups shredded Italian blend cheese (ensure no corn-derived starches or additives)
- 1/3 cup grated parmesan

**Directions:**
1. In a Dutch oven, cook the ground beef, chopped onion, chopped green pepper, and minced garlic over medium heat until the beef is browned and the vegetables are tender. Drain the excess grease.
2. Stir in the undrained crushed tomatoes, tomato sauce, drained mushrooms, sugar, oregano, salt, and basil. Bring the mixture to a boil, then reduce the heat and let it simmer, uncovered, for 20-25 minutes. Stir occasionally.
3. Remove the meat sauce from heat and stir in the drained spaghetti.
4. Place half of the spaghetti-meat sauce mixture into a 13x9x2 baking dish. Sprinkle with half of the shredded Italian blend cheese.
5. Top with the remaining spaghetti and meat sauce. Sprinkle with the grated parmesan cheese.
6. Bake the casserole in a preheated oven at 375 degrees Fahrenheit for 30 minutes, or until the cheese is bubbly and golden brown.
7. Remove from the oven and let it cool slightly before serving.

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

- Ensure that all canned products, such as the crushed tomatoes and tomato sauce, are verified to contain no corn-derived additives or cross-contamination. This includes avoiding items like citric acid and other preservatives that could be corn-based.
- Validate that the spaghetti is certified corn-free. Some pasta may use corn-based ingredients or have cross-contamination risks during production.
- Check that the shredded Italian blend cheese does not contain corn-derived starches or anticaking agents commonly used in pre-shredded cheese products.

Requirement: Mustard-free

The newly generated recipe is:

Modified Recipe for Pineapple Chess Pie

Ingredients:
- 1/2 cup unsalted butter
- 1 1/2 cup granulated sugar
- 4 large eggs
- 3 tbsp all-purpose flour
- 1 can (8 oz) crushed pineapple, drained
- 1 tsp pure vanilla extract
- 1 9" unbaked pie shell (deep dish)

Directions:
1. Preheat your oven to 350°F (175°C).
2. Lightly spray a pie dish with a non-stick cooking spray, and place the pie crust in the pie dish.
3. In a mixing bowl, cream together the unsalted butter and granulated sugar until well blended, for about one minute.
4. Add the eggs and all-purpose flour to the butter mixture, and beat well until the mixture is smooth.
5. Stir in the drained crushed pineapple and pure vanilla extract, mixing until well combined.
6. Pour the mixture into the prepared pastry shell.
7. Bake in the preheated oven for 45 minutes, or until the filling is set and the top is lightly golden.
8. Allow the pie to cool completely before serving. Enjoy!

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Baigan Choka Recipe**

**Ingredients:**
- 3 whole Large Eggplants
- 3 whole Plum Tomatoes
- 9 cloves Garlic
- 1 whole Medium Onion, Thinly Sliced
- 4 Tablespoons Extra Virgin Olive Oil (ensure sesame-free variety)
- Canola Oil, For Roasting Eggplant
- Fresh Hot Pepper, such as Scotch Bonnet, Habanero, or Jalapeno (optional)
- Salt, to taste

**Directions:**
1. Rub the eggplant with a little canola oil. Roast the vegetables over an open flame (either on a grill or directly on a gas stovetop) until the skins are charred and the vegetables are cooked. Let cool and peel the vegetables. Discard any extra liquid released.
   
2. Trim the stems off the eggplant. Chop the eggplant into pieces and put them in a bowl. Add the tomatoes and mash with a fork until there are no more chunks. Take the peeled garlic, mash it with a fork, and add it to the mixture along with the slices of onion. Season with salt and some fresh hot pepper, to taste.
   
3. Right before serving, heat up 3-4 tablespoons of sesame-free extra virgin olive oil with 2-3 smashed cloves of garlic. When the garlic starts sizzling, take off heat and pour over the eggplant mixture. Give it one more stir, and serve with roti or naan.

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

Ensure that the extra virgin olive oil used is explicitly labeled and certified sesame-free to avoid cross-contamination risks. Although the recipe states to use a sesame-free variety, it is crucial to verify that the oil does not have any traces of sesame, considering cross-reactivity and allergy concerns.

All other modifications made to the recipe align with the sesame-free requirement, and the cooking steps remain logical and feasible with the modified ingredients. However, the certification of the oil is a critical concern that must be resolved to safely meet the dietary restriction.

Case 191-Title: Rhonda'S Yeast Rolls
Ingredients: ["2 sticks butter", "2/3 c. sugar", "1 c. boiling water", "2 pkg. yeast", "2 Tbsp. lukewarm water", "6 to 7 c. plain flour", "1 c. cold water", "2 eggs, beaten", "2 tsp. salt"]
Directions: ["Follow steps exactly:", "Mix boiling water, sugar and margarine. Stir this until margarine melts.", "Dissolve yeast in lukewarm water. Add to sugar mixture.", "Add eggs, then flour.", "This will start to get stiff.", "Roll, cut or drop by spoonfuls in muffin pans.", "This needs to rise 2 hours in warm place.", "Brush with melted butter before baking.", "Bake at 450\u00b0 for 10 minutes."]
Requirement: Mustard-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Recipe for Rhonda's Yeast Rolls (Mustard-Free)**

Ingredients:
- 1 cup unsalted butter
- 2/3 cup sugar
- 1 cup boiling water
- 2 packages yeast (ensure yeast does not contain mustard derivatives)
- 2 tablespoons lukewarm water
- 6 to 7 cups plain all-purpose flour
- 1 cup cold water
- 2 large eggs, beaten
- 2 teaspoons salt

Directions:
1. Mix the boiling water, sugar, and unsalted butter in a large bowl. Stir until the butter melts completely.
2. In a small bowl, dissolve the yeast in lukewarm water. Let it sit for a few minutes until it becomes frothy, then add it to the sugar mixture.
3. Stir in the beaten eggs until well combined.
4. Gradually add the flour, mixing well after each addition. The dough will start to get stiff as you incorporate all the flour.
5. Once the dough is fully mixed, roll it out on a floured surface and cut it into pieces, or drop spoonfuls of dough into greased muffin pans.
6. Allow the rolls to rise in a warm place for about 2 hours or until doubled in size.
7. Preheat the oven to 450°F.
8. Brush the tops of the rolls with melted butter.
9. Bake in the preheated oven for 10 minutes or until golden brown.

Requirement: Egg-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Keepin' Slaw Recipe (Egg-Free)**

Ingredients:
- 1 medium head cabbage, shredded very fine
- 3/4 cup sugar
- 1 cup apple cider vinegar
- 3/4 cup sunflower oil
- 1 teaspoon celery seed
- 1 teaspoon salt
- 1 teaspoon dry mustard
- 2 teaspoons sugar
- 1 teaspoon onion powder
- 1/2 teaspoon turmeric

Directions:
1. Shred cabbage very fine and place in a large bowl.
2. Sprinkle the shredded cabbage with 3/4 cup sugar.
3. In a saucepan, combine apple cider vinegar, sunflower oil, celery seed, salt, dry mustard, 2 teaspoons sugar, onion powder, and turmeric. Bring the mixture to a boil.
4. Pour the hot mixture over the shredded cabbage.
5. Cover the bowl and place it in the refrigerator for 4 to 6 hours, or overnight for best results.
6. Before serving, mix the slaw thoroughly and drain excess liquid.
7. Serve chilled. The slaw keeps crisp in the refrigerator for up to a week.

Case 197-Title: Beef Stew
Ingredients: ["1/2 cup flour", "1 teaspoon salt", "1/4 teaspoon pepper", "2 pounds stew beef, cubed", "3 teaspoons olive oil or butter", "1 bay leaf", "1 clove garlic, smashed", "1 beef stock cube", "1 pound small onions", "6 carrots, sliced", "3 medium-size potatoes, quartered", "1 package frozen peas"]
Directions: ["Mix flour, salt, and pepper in a bowl and coat each piece of beef with it.", "Heat olive oil or butter in a heavy pot or Dutch oven and brown the meat over moderate heat.", "Remove meat as necessary to brown remaining meat.", "Return all meat to the pot.", "Dissolve beef stock cube in 2 cups boiling water and add to pot with meat.", "Add bay leaf and garlic and bring to a boil.", "Lower heat, cover, and simmer slowly until the meat is tender.", "Add onions, carrots, and potatoes; stir to mix ingredients, and cook for 10 minutes.", "Add peas, and continue simmering until the meat and vegetables are tender, about 20 minutes."]
Requirement: Wheat-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Wheat-Free Beef Stew**

**Ingredients:**
- 1/2 cup gluten-free all-purpose flour blend 
- 1 teaspoon salt
- 1/4 teaspoon pepper
- 2 pounds stew beef, cubed
- 3 teaspoons olive oil
- 1 bay leaf
- 1 clove garlic, smashed
- 1 gluten-free beef stock cube
- 1 pound small onions
- 6 carrots, sliced
- 3 medium-sized potatoes, quartered
- 1 package frozen peas

**Directions:**
1. Mix the gluten-free flour blend, salt, and pepper in a bowl and coat each piece of beef with it.
2. Heat olive oil in a heavy pot or Dutch oven and brown the meat over moderate heat.
3. Remove meat as necessary to brown the remaining meat.
4. Return all meat to the pot.
5. Dissolve the gluten-free beef stock cube in 2 cups of boiling water and add to the pot with the meat.
6. Add the bay leaf and garlic and bring to a boil.
7. Lower heat, cover, and simmer slowly until the meat is tender.
8. Add onions, carrots, and potatoes; stir to mix ingredients, and cook for 10 minutes.
9. Add peas, and continue simmering until the meat and vegetables are tender, about 20 minutes.

Case 198-Title: Gluten Free Cauliflower Kale Pesto Pizza
Ingredients: ["Cauliflower Pizza", "1 Small head cauliflower (about 3 cups)", "1 tablespoon Olive oil", "1 teaspoon Dry oregano", "1/8 teaspoon Chile flakes (optional)", "1/4 cup Water", "1 pint Cherry Tomatoes", "1 teaspoon Olive oil", "1/4 teaspoon Lemon zest", "1/2 Lemon juice only", "Kale Pesto", "1 bunch Kale leaves only packed tight (about 4 cups)", "1/4 cup Walnuts or pinenuts or pistachio (optional)", "1/4 cup Olive oil (extra if you like it creamier)", "1/4 cup Grated parmesan (optional) you can also use", "1/2 Lemon juice only", "Salt and pepper to taste"]

Requirement: Wheat-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Gluten Free Cauliflower Kale Pesto Pizza (Modified Recipe)**

**Ingredients:**

- Cauliflower Pizza Base:
  - 1 small head cauliflower (about 3 cups)
  - 1 tablespoon extra virgin olive oil
  - 1 teaspoon dried oregano
  - 1/8 teaspoon chile flakes (optional)
  - 1/4 cup water
  - 1/2 lemon, juiced
  - Salt and pepper to taste
- Toppings:
  - 1 pint cherry tomatoes
  - 1 teaspoon extra virgin olive oil
  - 1/4 teaspoon lemon zest
  - Salt and pepper to taste
  - Optional toppings: sliced olives, sautéed mushrooms, caramelized onions, roasted peppers
- Kale Pesto:
  - 1 bunch kale leaves only, packed tight (about 4 cups)
  - 1/4 cup walnuts or pine nuts or pistachios (omit for nut-free option)
  - 1/4 cup extra virgin olive oil (add extra if you like it creamier)
  - 1/4 cup nutritional yeast (for a nutty, cheesy flavor)
  - 1/2 lemon, juiced
  - Salt and pepper to taste

**Instructions:**

1. Preheat oven to 400°F.
2. Wash and cut the florets off a small head of cauliflower. Chop into small pieces and put in a Vitamix, powerful blender, or food processor with 1 tablespoon olive oil, 1 teaspoon oregano, 1/8 teaspoon chile flakes (if using), 1/2 lemon juiced, and 1/4 cup water. Blend until smooth.
3. Grease a pie pan by rubbing about 1 teaspoon olive oil on it or spraying it with a cooking spray. In a large pie pan or tart pan (about 10.5 inches) or on a baking sheet with parchment paper, spread out the puree in an even circle about 1/2 inch thick. Bake until golden on top, about 35 minutes.
4. For the tomatoes, get a baking sheet and line it with parchment paper. Add the olive oil, lemon zest, salt, and pepper. Bake until the tomatoes are wrinkled and popped, about 25 minutes.
5. When the cauliflower base is golden, turn off the oven for 15 minutes to dry out the crust.
6. Spread about half of the pesto on top of the cauliflower base. Add roasted tomatoes on top. Add optional toppings if desired, such as sliced olives, sautéed mushrooms, caramelized onions, or roasted peppers.
7. For the kale pesto, wash, dry, and de-stem the kale. Dry the kale leaves in a salad spinner. Add all pesto ingredients in a powerful blender or food processor.
8. Blend until it forms a thick paste using a plunger attachment if available or a rubber spatula to stir and blend well.
9. Taste and add salt and pepper to the kale pesto as needed, then blend again to incorporate the seasoning.
10. Store leftover pesto in the fridge for up to one week or freeze in 1/4 cup portions in mini Ziploc bags for quick defrosting and meals.

Case 199-Title: Cloverleaf Rolls
Ingredients: ["6 c. flour", "1/2 c. sugar", "1 tsp. salt", "2 pkg. dry yeast", "1 c. warm water", "1 c. warm milk", "1 stick soft butter", "1 egg, beaten"]
Directions: ["Combine 1/4 cup water, yeast and 1 teaspoon sugar.", "Combine flour, sugar and salt.", "Add to milk, water, egg and soft butter. Knead well, then let rise double in bulk."]
Requirement: Gluten-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Recipe: Gluten-Free Cloverleaf Rolls**

**Ingredients:**
- 6 cups gluten-free all-purpose flour blend (ensure it contains xanthan gum or add 1 tsp separately)
- 1/2 cup sugar
- 1 tsp salt
- 2 packets dry yeast (gluten-free certified)
- 1 cup warm water (110°F)
- 1 cup warm milk (use gluten-free and cow's milk-free option if needed, like almond or oat milk)
- 1 stick (1/2 cup) soft butter (ensure gluten-free; can substitute with dairy-free butter if necessary)
- 1 egg, beaten (or use a flax egg: 1 tbsp ground flaxseed mixed with 2.5 tbsp water)

**Directions:**
1. In a small bowl, combine 1/4 cup warm water, the yeast, and 1 teaspoon sugar. Stir gently and let sit for about 5 minutes until the mixture becomes foamy.
2. In a large mixing bowl, whisk together the gluten-free flour blend, remaining sugar, and salt.
3. Add the yeast mixture, remaining water, milk, beaten egg (or flax egg), and soft butter to the dry ingredients.
4. Mix until a smooth dough forms. If the dough is too sticky, add a tablespoon of flour at a time until it is manageable.
5. Knead the dough on a lightly floured surface (using gluten-free flour) for about 5-7 minutes until it is smooth and elastic.
6. Transfer the dough to a lightly greased bowl, cover with a damp cloth, and let it rise in a warm place until it has doubled in bulk, about 1 to 1.5 hours.
7. Preheat your oven to 350°F (175°C).
8. Punch down the dough and divide into small balls, about the size of a walnut. Place three balls into each cup of a greased muffin tin to create the cloverleaf shape.
9. Cover the rolls with a cloth and let them rise for another 15-20 minutes.
10. Bake in the preheated oven for about 15-20 minutes, or until the tops are golden brown.
11. Remove from oven and let cool slightly before serving. Enjoy warm.
